**URL:** https://akanyaburunga.wordpress.com/2024/12/25/kubera-iki-noweli-ihimbazwa-ku-wa-25-kigarama/

Yezu (Yesu) yaravutse, haciye imyaka irenga 2000. Ivuka ryiwe ryarahimbajwe kandi nâ€™ubu rikiriko, si agaseseshwarumuri. Mu mihingo yose yâ€™isi, mu bihugu bitandukanye eka na hano mu bwa Nyaburunga rirahimbazwa ukuri kwamye mu miryango yâ€™abakirisu nâ€™abagenzi babo. Mu bisagara no mu misozi isharije uburundi, hose haririmbwa â€œGloriaâ€, bisigura â€œumunezeroâ€. None mwoba muzi inkomoko yâ€™ihimbazwa ryâ€™uwo musiÂ ? Kubera iki hoho uhimbazwa kuri rino genekerezoÂ ? Tugira turabire hamwe amamuko yâ€™uwo musi nâ€™igenekerezo uhimbarizwako.
Amazina yâ€™uwo musi wama uhimbazwa kandi urindiranwa igishika uko umwaka utashe aratandukanye bivanye nâ€™abayakoresha, hamwe nâ€™imico yabo. Nko mu bihugu vyâ€™uburaruko bwa kure Sikandinaviya bawita Jul, ijambo bari basanganywe mu mico yabo ahubwo risigura ikiringo cose Noweli imara, hafu ukwazi kwose kwa Kigarama. Mu Budagi bawita Weihnachten, bisigura ijoro rihezagiye. Mu bihugu bikoresha indimi zo mu muryango wâ€™ikiromani hoho bawitirira ivuka, haba mu gitaliyano ( natale) mu giporotigare (natal) no mu gisupanyoro (navidad).

Iryo zina turikesha abakoroni bazanye idini, nabo bakaba bari ababiligi baturuka mu gace kavuga igifaransa, gutyo dutorana NoÃ«l.
Ku wa 25 Kigarama, vyaje gute ?Imbere yâ€™ivuka rya Yezu (Yesu), mu bice vya buraya hari hasanzwe umuco wo kwigina umuco inyuma yâ€™ikiringo kirekire haba hamaze ijoro riba rirerire umusi nawo ukaba mugufi, ikiringo ibihugu vyo mu buraruko bwâ€™isi biba biri mu mbeho nyinshi cane hakoroka nâ€™urubura. Ivyo bitumwa nâ€™uko isi iba iriko irihindukiza, ico gice câ€™isi kikaba kure yâ€™izuba, umuco ntunagishikire neza. Reka tureke kubanza kubajana muri birebire tugaruke ku kiyago cacu.
Abanyaburaya rero uwo musi bari basanzwe bawuhimbaza kuva kera cane, bakabikora ugutandukanye, bigina uwo muco ugarutse, iryo zuba rinesheje umuzimiza.
Aho hose barashariza ubujwari, bakatsa amatara, bakagira imisi mikuru idasanzwe.Kugaruka ku ka kera
Mu kinjana ca kane ( IV) inyuma yâ€™ivuka rya Yezu, ni ho umwami wâ€™abami Konstantino na Papa Liberiyo biga umukenyuro wâ€™ukuntu abantu bokwijukira guhimbaza Noweli cane, niko guca bawuhuza nâ€™imico kama kâ€™ivyo bihugu, bagafatira kuri ya misi twababwira aho hejuru bari basanzwe bakunda guhimbaza, ni uko umusi wa 25 Kigarama uba urafashwe. ## Vyinshi ku mugenzo woÂ kuraguza
**Date:** January 13, 2017 8:21 am  
**URL:** https://akanyaburunga.wordpress.com/2017/01/13/vyinshi-ku-mugenzo-wo-kuraguza/

Ukuraguza vyararanze uburundi kuva kera na rindi. Vyatumwa nâ€™ibintu vyinshi mu buzima bwâ€™abarundi zaba ingorane canke ineza. Ibikoresho vyakoreshwa muri uwo mugenzo navyo ntivyari bisanzwe nkâ€™uko tugomba tubibashikireko uko twabitohoje.
Ishusho:commons.wikimedia.org
Ntitwoshobora kuvuga kuraguza tutavuze gupfumura. Ivyo bikorwa vyama biri kumwe na ntaryo. Iyo umuntu araguje, ni uko haba hariho uwundi ariko arapfumura. Gupfumura navyo bigirwa nâ€™umupfumu. Uwo nawe ni umuntu aragura, avuga ingorane zabaye canke izizoba. Akamaro kâ€™umupfumu kandi kwari ugukingira abantu nkâ€™ibirozi mu kubambika ibiheko Â canke akabaha umuti. Imiti yatanga yari ubwoko bwinshi, hari nâ€™iyo uwaraguza atamenya. Yaratanga imirogoro, umurigatano, agasabirwa, nâ€™iyindi. Iyo yose yari ifise ico ivura nâ€™ico ayitangira.
Ni ryari abarundi bitura abapfumu?
Abarundi ntayandi mirukiro bari bafise. Abapfumu nibo baganga bari bahari. Icaba cose kiraba ubuzima bwâ€™umuntu, baca bitura umupfumu. Kenshi bamwitura iyo bari mu ngorane. Bashobora kumwitura iyo umwana ashushe. Iyo inka yanse kwima, umuryango wagumbashe canke umukobwa yatevye kuronka umugabo, canke nyene hagatera ikiza mu muryango baraja kubaza umupfumu. Cari co kimwe nâ€™iyo umuntu kanaka abuze uwiwe.
Eka nâ€™iyo batari mu ngorane, baritura umupfumu kuko bamana ubwoba kandi bategerezwa kuguma bitegeyeko. Kanatsinda ntawumenya iyo ruzanana.Â  Nâ€™uwaba agomba kwubaka urwâ€™iwe yaraja kubaza rumenyi akamuha agaheko kazomukingira mu mugerero mushasha. Yaranabaza uko bazobana nâ€™uwo muntu mushasha, bakereranira.
Ibitahara muri uwo mugirwa
Bagiye kuraguza batwara ivyo bita â€œibimaziâ€. Ivyo navyo kera vyari ibiribwa canke ibintu vyâ€™agaciro kanini Â (ibirezi, ibihete, imiringa, â€¦) bajana kugire umupfumu ashobore kurangura neza akazi kiwe.Â  Aho abazungu baziye bakazana amafaranga, ibimazi vyarahindutse bicika amafaranga. Uwaja kuraguza rero yaca atwara amafaranga. Ayo rero ni ivyero uwuraguza yatanga ngo umupfumu amuragurira amwereze. Igihe umuntu yaragiriwe neza (Imana ikamuha) yaratanga â€œintasuroâ€, kari agashimwe kâ€™intungwa canke ikindi kintu yaha umupfumu nkâ€™agashimweinyuma yâ€™uko yamukingiye Imana ikamutaka ivyiza.
Inyambaro yâ€™umupfumu nayo yari ihambaye cane. Ntiyapfa kwambara uko ashatse kwose kuko yaba ari ku kazi gahambaye. Nka kurya nâ€™abaganga bâ€™ubu bose bafise umwambaro ubatandukanya, umwe wese kuco ashoboye, umupfumu yaba yambaye urushato rwâ€™ingwe nâ€™intutu (inkofero) ikozwe mu rushato rwâ€™inkende.Â  Hejuru yararenzako ibiheko vyinshi nko mwâ€™izosi, ku maboko canke ku maguru.
Hari ibikoresho bitahara. Umupfumu yategerezwa kuba afise na ntaryo urunyagara, akarende karumirijemwo utubuye canke imbuto zâ€™umugunguma yaja arajegeza (kuvuza urunyagara) igihe cose agire avuge ikintu abwiwe nâ€™â€œabavyeyiâ€ nkâ€™uko bivugwa. Ikindi kintu yategerezwa kuba afiseÂ  ni inkoronko, nyankobwa mu gihe ari umugore canke Nyabusorongo mu gihe ari umugabo. Utwo natwo ni uturende twaba dufise uburunga ku mutwe( kuri Nyabusorongo); nâ€™ubuyeye (kuri Nyankobwa). Hari nâ€™ibindi bikoresho vyinshi baba bafise nkâ€™udukono two guteka imiti nâ€™ibindi.
None abapfumu bari abangushi?
Kurya kwâ€™ibindi bikorwa vyose bikora ku buzima bwâ€™abantu, utunenge ntitwobura. Irya nyambaro yonyene yari iteye ubwoba kugire abantu bamutinye ivyo avuze bavyemere badahingitanya. Ikindi naco, umupfumu yarashobora kwihenda akavuga ibitari vyo, akabivuga uko avyiyumvira canke mu kuvura agacacisha. Hari nâ€™abaca bica umwuga mu kuwufatanya no kurogaÂ ; aho gufasha umuntu akamuha ibitari vyo. Abarozi barabakoresha mu kwica abo batoshikiriye arivyo bita Â«Â kuguraÂ Â». Umupfumu baramuha ibitagenda mpaka yemeye akica umuntu bamuguzeko.
Ariko hari abapfumu babikorana akarangamutima kadasanzwe bakagira ico bamariye abarundi. Ni naho wama usanga nkâ€™umuryango wose wifitiye umupfumu wagenzuye ukama uja kuraguza ko, kuko baba baramushimye ko ari nâ€™umutima. Niho wasanga hari abantu bava impinga bakaza ku mupfumu kanaka. Bari bazi ko barushanya umutima nâ€™ubushobozi kandi bategerezwa kuja kure kugire bashike iyo abansi batoshika.
Kuraguza vyari bifise ikibanza kinini mu kwemera kwâ€™abarundi. Imana Rugiravyose bari bazi kandi ko ica kuri Kiranga mu kubaha imihezagiro, eka mbere no ku bapfumu kugire baburire abantu hanyuma bitegereko Rwuba ntibahekure. Niho wasanga kenshi umupfumu aragurira umuntu guterekera. Nâ€™iyo habaye ikintu kibi mu muryango baraja kwa rumenyi kugire bamenye icatumye biba hanyuma bagaterekera.
Ubiravye neza usanga umupfumu yari afise ikibanza gisumba ica Kiranga. Igikorwa ca Kiranga nyamukuru kwari ukurongora ibisabisho vyâ€™abarundi akabishikana ku Mana. Atari ubwo bushobozi bwonyene, ahandi yaboneka nkâ€™umuntu nkâ€™abandi. Ariko umupfumu wewe yari atinyitse rwose, kuko yabona ubuzimwa bwâ€™umuntu wese amwituye.Â  Ikindi naco, ni uko umwami atigera yitura kiranga kuko yavuga ngo ni mwenewabo (vyumvikana ko boba bangana) ariko yaba afise abapfumu benshi cane baguma bamurabira ubuzima bwiwe nâ€™ubwâ€™igihugu.

â€œIyo aba iyo ngabire bafise boyikoresheje mu biteza imbere imico, ururimi nâ€™akaranga vyacu wosanga babikoze neza cane nâ€™ururimi rwacu rukifatira abantu kuko ijwi ryabo rishika kure.â€

**Date:** January 9, 2025 7:30 pm

Umurisho wâ€™Ingoma ni intambo iryoheye ijisho Uburundi bwirata iwabwo eka mbere no mu makungu. Mu kuzivuza no mu kuzitamba, abatimbo ari bo bahebera bihebeye Ingoma bagira ibimenyetso vyinshi, bagakora nâ€™iyindi migirwa ibiherekeza.Â  Umutama Duniya Abedi yaradutsatsuriye ku vyo azi ku murisho wâ€™ingoma yatanguye kuvuza agifise imyaka 11 mu mwaka wâ€™1982 gushika ubu. Reka umunyakaranga MpunduYera abacire ku mayange bimwe muri vyo yatwegeranirije ; nta nkeka ko vyobagirira akamaro namwe.
Hari mu giteramo ngarukakwezi Rinjora cabayeÂ  kwâ€™igenekerezo rya 27 Kigarama 2024, ica nyuma casozereye uwo mwaka. Imbere yâ€™isinzi ryâ€™Abarundi bâ€™ingeri zose, uwo munyakaranga yabigize umwuga yatubwiye vyinshi ku ngoma abari bahari twese turajorerwa.
Ubwa mbere na mbere, twamenye ko igikoresho ndangakaranga citwa Ingoma kugira kiboneke habwirizwa kuba hakoranijwe ibintu bitatu : igiti câ€™umuvugangoma, kiba kimaze nâ€™imiburiburi hagati yâ€™imyaka 100 nâ€™150 ; ubworozi bwâ€™inka, kuko ata ngoma yoboneka itagira icahi, naco kikaba ari urusato rwâ€™inka rwo kuyikana hamwe rero nâ€™umuntu ubwiwe kuko ari we akora ivyo bikorwa vyose gushika agere kuvuza ingoma.
Ikimenyetso câ€™intwaro
Ingoma kandi ni icitiranwa câ€™Ubutegetsi canke Intwaro. Niho uzokwumva ngo â€œhari ku ngoma ya Mwezi, ya Mutaga canke iya Mwambutsaâ€¦â€
Duniya yatwiganiye ko ingoma ziranga uko igihugu gitunganijwe canecane mu ntwaro, akabisigura ati:
Ingoma harya bazishize ku mutwe bagaca bazitambukira ari vyo bita kwirungera bisigura ubutegetsi bugendagenda mu gihugu ;
Kubera ubutegetsi bushobora guhungabanywa, ni co gituma zigenda ziyobowe nâ€™inkinzo nâ€™icumu vyo gukinga no kwivuna uwoshaka guhungabanya ubutegetsi ;
Ingoma iyo bazivyagije hasi baca urya mudiho nâ€™umuhamirizo wâ€™ingoma, baba bashaka gusigura ko ata muntu aza kudurumbanya ubutegetsi. Niho rero baca batera umuhamirizo incuro zitatu kugira barabe ko ata mwansi yinyegeje hafi babonye ata we baca batangura rero kwigina no gushinga amategeko. Aho hose uwufise icumu nâ€™inkinzo aguma agavye kuko ata kwijajara.
Duca tuhamenyera nâ€™ibindi vyinshi
Ibindi Â yaciye atwiganira mu kiyago camaze isaha yose ni uko muri iyi ntambo yâ€™ingoma, ikintu cose kigira insiguro kandi ikomeye, uhereye ku ngoma ubwayo
Irya ngoma igendera imbere isize amabara yâ€™igihugu bayita inkiranya ;
Muri make izi ngoma zâ€™abahebera bihebeye ingoma zerekana uko igihugu cari gitunganijeÂ muÂ vyâ€™intwaro.
Ariko rero ikiyago carinze gihera abatari bake badashizwe, bafise ibibazo vyinshi bikeneye inyishu kandi bamwe basaba ko yogaruka bakayaga kugira ikiyago kibandanye kinonosorwa cane. Mu Burundi, ibigize imico nâ€™imigenzo biriko birazimangana si kimwe kandi si bibiri. Duhereye ku nyambaro, tukaja ku bifungurwa, tukaja no mu mayagwa, hari vyinshi bias nâ€™ibiriko biribagirwa hakaba nâ€™ivyamaze kugenda burundu. Akarorero ka hagufi ni akazÃªhÃ©, ubuhinga bwo kuramukanya bwari bwiharijwe nâ€™abakenyezi, ubu kibagiwe, gasigaye kavuzwa mu maradiyo ariko kavuye mu kubaho kwâ€™Abarundi. Twashimye kukagarukako.
Mu binyamakuru, kino gihe haguma hagaruka ko akazÃªhÃ© kibagiwe, kandi ko gakwiye kugarukirwa. Aho ni mu gihe abatohoji no mu migwi ndangakaranga na nyuramico, bo babona ko ico kintu cagaragaza ubumwe no kubana neza, hamwe nâ€™igishika incuti zifitaniye biriko birazimangana, ahubwo bikwiriye kugarukirwa.
Ntibarira busema kuko haba mu bakuru, haba mu bato, iyo ndamutso yaribagiwe mu 2025. Nâ€™iyo ivugijwe mwâ€™iradiyo canke igakoreshwa mu bikino nyuramico canke mu masabukuru, bikorwa kugira abantu bibutse aka kera gusa, ariko akazÃªhÃ© karamaze kuva mu bikorwa iyo abakenyezi canke umuvyeyi nâ€™umwana bahuye baramukanya.
Muti none akazÃªhe ni ikiÂ ?
Akazehe canke akayego ariko gahibongozo ni uburyo bwo kuramukanya bwiharijwe nâ€™abakenyezi (nâ€™abigeme), aho abaramukanya bahibongoza baterera mu gahogo, maze bakaganira bahuza, babazanya bishurana ku buzima babayemwo. Bashobora kumara iminota yababa itanu baguhoberanye bongera bahibongoza.
Abaramukanya barabanza bakarabana mu maso bagaragaza igishika nâ€™inkumbu bafitaniye, mu nyuma ba gahoberana bakaguma babumbatiranye, uwundi mwanya baja barahinduranya, begerana baja i buryo, i bubamfu gutyo gutyo nkâ€™incuro cumi. Hari nâ€™aho bahagarika bakaguma babumbatiranye. Umwe atera, uwundi yitabiriza, barakiranwa. Igihe cose mu kazehe hatangura gutera uwisumbuye mu myaka mu bariko bararamukanya. Ikindi naco, ni uko akazehe kama gaherezwa no gukorana mu ntoke (guhana yambu mu mvugo yâ€™ubu). Ivyo bikorwa ku baba ari incuti, canke abasanzwe ari ababanyi bashize hamwe, eka mbere nâ€™umuvyeyi nâ€™umwana bararamukanya mu kazÃªhÃ©. Bapfa kuba bazinanye neza gusa.
Nkâ€™uko Isaac Ndimurwanko yabigaragaje, ayo ni amasano cumi yâ€™ivyiyumviro bikurikirana mu majambo yâ€™Akazehe. Ashobora kwerekana :
Intara uwo mugenzo wari waragumijwe bimwe biboneka, nkâ€™uko abatohoji babivuze, ni intara ya Ngozi mu makomine yayo atandukanye.
Mu bintu Abarundi bavuga ko vyatumye uwo mugenzo ugabanuka, harimwo amagume igihugu caciyemwo na canecane mu myaka yâ€™1990 hamwe nâ€™ibi biza bija biraduka bibuza abantu kwegerana nâ€™igishika harimwo koronavirusi.

## â€œGiciyeâ€Â : haca igikiÂ ? Iryo jambo risiguraÂ iki?
**Date:** March 8, 2024 9:17 pm  
**URL:** https://akanyaburunga.wordpress.com/2024/03/08/giciye-haca-igiki-iryo-jambo-risigura-iki/

Mu mvugo yâ€™Ikirundi, na canecane mu mvyino zâ€™agahogo kâ€™abarundi, turamenyereye kwumva mu bitero bashiramwo ngo â€œ ngende giciyeâ€, â€œturagenda giciyeâ€, â€¦. Abarutse ubu riradusiga, kuko hari nâ€™ayandi majambo tudashoka dutahura avugwa mu Kirundi. None iryo jambo ryoba risigura iki? Ico gica coco ni igiki? Tubasabikanirize insiguro twahawe nâ€™abakurambere twayaze.
Ku batararyomva, bokwumviriza uruvyino rwakunzwe cane rwâ€™umugwi ndangakaranga Higa, rwavyinywe nâ€™abana bakiri bato ico gihe rwitwa Yoronimu. Muri urwo ruvyino, iryo jambo ryarakoreshejwe. No mu ruvyino rwa Giramahoro, Ngoma ya Ruhinda, iryo jambo ryarakoreshejwe.
Uwatumye dukora aya matohoza kuri iryo jambo, ni uko hari uwagize amakenga ko barya bana mu buto bwabo batatahura amajambo bariko baravuga yose. Ko abarikoresheje boba baratahura insiguro yaryo, si co tuja kurabira hamwe. Bararirimvye, badutuma dukurira mu karanga kandi twumva akadiho kâ€™iwacu banabuza amajamboi amwe amwe adapfa. Mbega iyo batarikoresha tuba turiko tuganira kuki?
None ico gica ni igiki?
Mu Burundi, ibikorwa bihuza abantu bakaja hamwe nko kuvyina no gutamba, bisanzwe bihabwa ikibanza kinini cane mu biruhura umuntu naho yoba afise ikimudundumiye ku mutima. Aho hambere rero, abantu barÄƒrama ku nama abakiri bato bagatamba cane bidagadura, bakikura ibinyugunyugu cane.
No mu migirwa yo kubandwa no guterekera, ivyigwa vyarerekanye ko hari ibintu vyafasha umuntu atamerewe neza afise ibigummbagumba canke ibiroroge vyamurengeye, bamubandiwe bikagabanya uburemere, agakira.
Ntiwtokwibagira kandi ko Abarundi baha ikibanza kinini kuyaga, kunywana bimwe bikwiye, ivyo bigatumwa no kugenderanira, baranayamaze ko agafuni kabagara ubumwe ari akarenge.
â€œIkigumbagumbaâ€ canke â€œikirorogeâ€
Ku bwâ€™umukurambere twayaze, ico gica rero ni ikigumbagumba kiba canize umuntu, iyo yidagaduye rero bikwiye abishizeko umutwe nâ€™umutima, nta kibuza ko gica, akumva icari ku mutima kirururutse. Icari kimudundumiye kubera kubura uwo mwanya wo kwidagadura, ushobora kuba ari umwitwarariko nâ€™ibindi, bica bigabanuka umuntu akaruhuka. Baca bavuga ngo â€œkiraciyeâ€.
Aha, uwoturusha gutohoza yotubariza ko hamwe bavuga ngo turabica bicike vyoba babikuye ngâ€™aho. Nta kiravyemeza dufise kuko uwo mukurambere twayaze we yaravyemeje ariko akekeranya.
Ikindi kivugwa, ni ikiroroge. Muti ico naco ni igikiÂ ? Ni urukumbuzi rwa cane, inkumbu nyinshi ugirira icuti canke umuvukanyi. Iyo zabaye umiurengera, zirahagarara ku mutima wâ€™umuntu akumva umenga zigiye kumuniga. Niho mu mvyino Â zindi twumva ibitero ngo â€œikiroroge kiranigaâ€.
Abandi nabo bati ni â€œigicuguâ€
Uwundi mukurambere nawe avuga ko nyabuna ikivugwa muri iyo mvugo ari igicugu. Ico naco ni igihe câ€™umusi kiri mu mwanya wâ€™ijoro, igihe kirenganye abantu baca batangura kuvyuka bifatira ingendo kugira izuba rimene ijuru banzaganije imisozi. Abo baba ari abafise ingendo. Uwo, avuga ko muri izo mvyino zose, bavuga ko baterama bagataha igicugu giciye, muri make, batahe bukeye kubera bahimbawe.
Nkako, mu ruvyino â€œIyo ntambaâ€ rwâ€™umugwi ndangakaranga Giramahoro, hoho baratomora neza mu gatero kagira indwi, bavuga bati: â€œigicugu kiraciye, ntamba weâ€. Aho turumva neza rukozi rwakoreshejwe ko ari igicugu cavuzwe.
Izo nsiguro zose uzumvirije usanga ari zo, ku buryo womenga ni rya jambo rimwe risigura menshi. Ariko iritomoye neza ryoba ryoroshe gutahurika ni irivuga igicugu kuko aho hambere abantu bagiye kuramukanya, baranywa bagatamba, bagataha bukeye canke butanguye kwenzura. Kira noneho, nâ€™ikiyago kibaye kirekire kiba caryoshe, iyo hariko hayaga abasanganywe: incuti, abavukanyi, umwana na nyina.

Aho hambere hahiseÂ twarashaza
Bayaga ntiyamenye ingene bashitse kwa sekuru, kuko ico kiyago cari camuryoheye cane. Asanga bavyarawe muÂ  rugo, bararamukanya. Yitera mu nzu kwa sekuru, inakuru aramuramutsa, aramuzimana. Bayaga yari yatamariwe nâ€™ivyo inakuru yambaye. Yatevye atiÂ : Â«Â Mbe nyoku, nkâ€™ivyo vyose wabikuye heÂ Â»Â ? Inakuru aratwenga ati:Â Â«Erega mwananje, na none agaciwe karuma, hambere aho twarashaza. Ibi ubona mwâ€™izosi, ni ubusaro nâ€™ibirezi. Hari nâ€™ibindi bininibinini abashingantahe bashazamwo, ari vyo bihete. Ibihete wumva, aho vyava ntawuhazi neza. Ariko bamwe bavuga ko vyaseswa nâ€™uruzi, bikaza bisa nâ€™imiruka yâ€™ibifyera, bikangana nâ€™ibakure, bikitwa ibirungu. Abandi bavuga ko vyava mubinono vyâ€™inzovu. Ibihete vaboneka bigoranye rwose. Ico vyavamwo cose vyagurwa vyinshi cane. Igihete gisenye neza carazimba, cagurwa inka nyishi kikambarwa nâ€™abaganwa nâ€™abatunzi. Bariko barasatura ibihete bongera babikarisha, haja haracagukako ibisate. Ivyo bisate ni vyo bakarishamwo ibirezi nkâ€™ibi nambaye. Ibirezi rero ni nkâ€™ibihete bitoyi. Barabitungira ku murya canke ku muhivu, abakenyezi bakavyambara mwâ€™izosi, hari uwambara bibiri, hari uwambara bibiri, hari uwambara bitatu, bine canke na bitanu.Na vyonyene vyagugwa inka. Umugabo yavyambika umugore, yaba yifise.
Bayaga abwira inakuru ati: Â«None ko ivyâ€™ibirezi nâ€™ivy,ibihete ndavyumvise,ibi vyo wambaye ku maboko ni ibikiÂ» ?
-Aha kumaboko nambaye imiringa nâ€™inyerere, no ku maguru ziruzuye. Imiringa yava mu butare bakura mu kuzimu. Abacuzi ni bo bayigurisha. Yambarwa nâ€™abagabo nâ€™abagore. Uko yarushanya ubwoko, niko yarushanya nâ€™igiciro. Ariko imiringa yâ€™abagabo ntiyangana nâ€™iyâ€™abagore. Abagabo bambara imiringa mininiminini ifise amazuru. Bayaga aca abaza inakuru ati: Â«None inyerere na zo zakorwa nâ€™abacuziÂ»?
-Ego, na zo nyene ni bo bazizinga, bazikura mu butare. Mukuzizinga, bakoresha ivyuma vyasigaye mu gucura imiringa. Barabikwega bikavamwo urutahe rurerure rwirabura canke rusa nâ€™umujumbu. Urwo ni rwo bazingira ku bushenza bwâ€™inka, bwâ€™impene canke ku bugwegwe, rukaba urunyerere. Izo nyerere zasa nâ€™intahe kandi zambarwa na bose, abagore nâ€™abagabo. Zashorwa nâ€™abayangayanga. ## Amajwi yâ€™ibikoko muÂ Kirundi
**Date:** June 24, 2022 11:16 pm  
**URL:** https://akanyaburunga.wordpress.com/2022/06/24/amajwi-yibikoko-mu-kirundi/

Mu rurimi rwacu, hari amavuga akoreshwa iyo igikoko iki canke kiriya gisohoye ijwi. Ayo rero ntasa kuri kimwe nâ€™ikindi. Mu rurimi rwâ€™Ikirundi, igikoko cose cisangiza irivuga rivuga imvugo yaco. Ngâ€™aya amwe muri yo.
Inka
Duhereye ku nka, igitungwa cubashwe cubashwe cane mu mateka yâ€™igihugu. Amavuga ni: kwaÃ bira, kuboroga, kuroha (igira irwane), kuvumera (iyo irondera inyana yayo ngo iyonse), kwivuga (impfizi), gupfuha.
ak.: Yabigoro iriko irabira, iraboroga, iravumera; nayo Rwamaza iriko irivuga, iravumeza, iraroha.
Imbwa
Ikindi gitungwa cari cari cubashwe mu Burundi. Nayo hakora amavuga: gukuga , kubweja, kugwangwara, kumoka.
ak.: Mugina iriko irakuga, irabweja, iragwangwara, iramoka.
Impene (ihene)
Iki ni ikindi gitungwa cororwa cane. Kwabira, guhebebeza, kuboroga (isuguru iriko ishaka kwimya imvyazi).
Intama
Iyi nayo, co kimwe nâ€™ihene, amavuga ni Kwabira, kuboroga.
Imbeba, inyoni, uduswi
Kujwiragira
Inkoko
Gukokoza, kubika, kwanira (iyo ibangamiwe),guteterera (yimirije guta amagi).
Imbwebwe
Kumoka
Intare
Kuroha
Nkâ€™uko mubibona, hari amajwi avugwa kumwe nko kuboroga mu gihe igikoko kigeramiwe ; kuroha mu gihe kigomba kurwana nâ€™ikindi, kwanira mu gihe bagira bagice izosi. Ayo majwi hari nâ€™ayo bisangiye nâ€™abantu.
Hakaba hari ayandi majwi tutavuze, yadusabikanirize.

## Amazina amwe amwe yâ€™ibiterwa muÂ Burundi

Mu Burundi, ibiti vyose biba bifise akamaro. Bishobora kuba ibiterwa birimwa maze bikera bakimbura bagafungura. Bishobora kandi kuba ibiti vyifashishwa mu bindi bikorwa nko kwubaka, gucana, nâ€™ibindi. â€œSlt! Aka kanimeroÂ  sinzi uwakampaye, nashaka kubamenyaâ€¦.â€; â€œMbega burya ndakuzi hehe sista? Aho hambere ho ntivyari uko. Umukobwa kugira utebe ubone uramushikiriye muganire waba wagiye gutega ku nzira ija kuvima Â imyaka nâ€™iyindi; waranditse amakete amwe ashika ayandi adashika ( aho hari ku bize) canke mbere warakeje inkere nkâ€™uko benshi babivuga.

Abantu benshi bakundana mu bihe biheze baba bahuriye kwâ€™ishure. Abatize nabo benshi ngo bahurira kwâ€™isengero canke kwâ€™isoko. Ngo no ku masengero kwari uko nyene. Barasenga imisa yâ€™abiyoga (imisa ya kabiri) hanyuma bagaca bahura isohotse ikiyago kikaba umunoni ingo zigashingwa zikaguma.

Akagenda akagaruka atavuze icamujanye.
Igikorwa câ€™Umuranzi
Co kimwe no mu myaka ya kera, nâ€™imbere yâ€™umuzo wâ€™uduhamagazo ngendanwa umuranzi yari afise ikibanza kidasanzwe mu guhuza imiryango. Nâ€™uwâ€™ubwoba nta ngorane yagira iyo yaciye ku muranzi.

Aha abâ€™ubu bacaniriwe cane baca bafata agahamagazo bakandika canke bagahamagara abo baba baramarana irungu, abandi bobo ntiboroherwa.Â  Baca bagenda ahantu bazi bahora bahurira nâ€™abakobwa nko ku nzira iva kwâ€™isoko kuvoma, kwâ€™ishure canke kwâ€™isengero; bakaraba ko hari uwo bobona baba baramenesha ibintu yikoreye canke bakaba barasororera ijisho nkâ€™uko umutama umwe yabimbwiye.
Mu gisagara, abo twayaze bambwiye ko bitari vyoroshe. Naho kubera inzira zaba zuzuye abahita benshi, kandi hari uruja nâ€™uruza rwinshi, ngo baja ku rupangu bazi ko hari umukobwa. Bagakora ibishoboka vyose bakamutora atawo mu rupangu wundi abiciye nâ€™ikanda. Nâ€™iyo umukobwa mwamenyanye ntivyoroha ko muhana isango.
None babikora bate?

Ku vyerekeye ugukundana kwiwe ( copinage) biratwengeje cane nkâ€™uko avyivugira.Â  â€œ Natanguye kuresha mfise imyaka mike cane. Nari aga smart boy.Â  Umukobwa twavugana rimwe nagenda yanyemeye. Ivyo vyabaye imbere gatoya yâ€™uko uduhamagazo ngendanwa tuza. Ngo kenshi babikora bamaze kuvugana nâ€™umukobwa. Nkâ€™iyo bigana canke basenga hamwe. ## Amajambo abarundi bakunda gukoresha bipfurizanya umwakaÂ mushasha
**Date:** January 30, 2018 12:43 pm  
**URL:** https://akanyaburunga.wordpress.com/2018/01/30/amajambo-abarundi-bakunda-gukoresha-bipfurizanya-umwaka-mushasha/

Uko imyaka yagiye iragenda, abarundi bagiye barahindura uko bipfurizannya umwaka mushasha. Ivyo vyatumwe nâ€™uko ukwemera, iminsi hamwe nâ€™ubuzima vyagiye birahinduka. Mu giteramo câ€™icuramayagwa co kuwa 10 nzero 2018, mu kigo ndangakaranga Â«Â Bwenge nyabwoÂ Â», abanyamuryango wâ€™akanyaburunga barateramanye bihweza amajambo amwe amwe abarundi bakoresha mu kwipfurizanya umwaka mushasha. Soma ico bashitseko.
Ishusho: flickr.com
Kwipfuriza umuntu kubaho neza, kuroranirwa, kugira amagara meza,â€¦. Â biba canke bitaba, abarundi ivyo ntubibabaza, barabikora ukuri kwamye. Babikora bizeye ko bitegerezwa kuba nkâ€™uko bavyipfuza, nkâ€™uko bavyemera. Vyose biba muri rwipfuriza, biherekejwe nâ€™ukwemera kwinshi. Ugasanga vyabaye umugenzo. Gurtyo, abarundiÂ  bo mu mihingo yose, barahuriza ku migirwa nâ€™imvugo zitari nke mu kwipfurizanya umwaka mushasha, muguhana ihobe.
Aho hambereâ€¦
Umwaka wâ€™aho hambere ntiwari ufatiye ku kwemera kwa gikirisu nko mu bihe vya none. Kanatsinda ivyo abarundi ntavyo bari bwamenye. Imbere yâ€™umuzo wâ€™abazugu, abarundi bari bafise ukwemera gushemeye cane, gufatiye ku buzima bwari buhari. Uko kwemera kwâ€™abasokuru kwari gushingiye ku bintu bitari bike harimwo nâ€™ibibiÂ : imizimu, intezi, nâ€™ibindi. Iyo umwaka utanguye, bafata ibibi bakavyipfuriza abansi, ivyiza navyo bakavyipfuriza abakunzi.
Senaka niwe yatanga umwaka kuri bose. Iyo atahari, uwuserukira umuryango niwe yawutanga. Akavuga amajambo akurikiraÂ : Â«Â Akira umwaka, tuwurye ntuturye. Uwawudutegeyemwo aze awuheremwo.Â Â». Vyumvikana ko umwansi bamwipfuriza kumererwa nabi, gushika nâ€™uko yopfaÂ : awuheremwo. Â Ivyo vyaba kenshiÂ : ku muganuro, ku cimburo canke ikindi gihe bashobora kwita umwaka.
Umwe mu bo twari kumwe Nsengiyumva, yaratubwiye ko ivyo yabibonyeÂ : Â«Â  Jewe nyene, ndibuka umubanyi ariko aratwipfuriza umwaka mwiza, hanyuma agaca adondagura amazina yâ€™abantu bose yikeka ko ari abansi biwe, akabahonyora hasi nkâ€™uko boba ariyo bari, akabasiribanga avuga ngo â€˜murakawuheramwo mweseâ€™.Â Â». Aho yavuga hari mu myaka ya mirongo icenda. Aho biraboneka ko mu mirongo ibiri canke imbere yaho hoho vyasumba aho.
Ubu ho guteÂ ?
Amajambo yagumye agaruka niÂ : Umwaka mushasha mwiza, umwaka muhire, tuwurye ntuturye, uzotubere uwâ€™amata nâ€™ubuki, uwâ€™amasaka nâ€™amasakaramento, uzowuronkemwo ivyo wipfuza vyoseâ€¦
Kuva ukwemera guhinyanyuwe, abarundi ntibavuye ku mugenzo wabo woguhana ihobe. Ariko vyarateye intambwe. Umwaka mushasha wararonse irindi genekerezo uberako, kuwa mbere Nzero. Mu kwipfurizanya umwaka mushasha mwiza, Â haravuyemwo ukwipfuriza inabi abandi. Ubu, umuntu apfuma amwipfuriza guhinduka ariko ntavuge ngo uwugwemwo. Amajambo yagumye ari yayandi, ariko hongeramwo imbabazi, ubuntu, amahoro, nâ€™akanyamuneza yahoranye. Ibitahoraho.
Abari bakoraniye aho twahana ivyiyumviro, baradushikirije umwe wese uko bawipfurizanya, mu ntara aturukamwo. Aho bavuga ikirundi kitavanze, bawipfurizanya kumweÂ :Â«Â Umwaka mushasha, uzotubere uwâ€™amata nâ€™ubuki, amahoro nâ€™amahonda. Tuzowuronkemwo ivyo twipfuza vyose, nâ€™amagara meza.Â Â». Kuva kuri Gerevazi aturuka mu bweru, Nsengiyumva aturuka mu bugesera, Nimubona akomoka mu Bututsi, nâ€™abandi bose, ayo majambo barayahurijeko.Â  Nivyo harongerako ayandi majambo bivanye nâ€™ibiraje ishinga umuryango nko kumenya mwâ€™ishure, Â ukuronka ikibondo, ugutsinda urubanza muri sentare,â€¦ ariko vyinshi barabihurizako.
Abari aho bose baremeza ko kwipfurizanya umwaka mushasha ari umugenzo mwiza. Bavuze ko ayo majambo bakoresha akomeye cane. Ameze nkâ€™igisabisho, gitera ubwira mu bikorwa. Nyamukuru, ni nkâ€™indagano yâ€™umubano mwiza.
Ico baneguye ni ingendo urwaruka rwatoye yo kubikora mu zindi ndimiÂ : igifaransa, icongereza, nâ€™ibindi. Navyo si bibi ngo ariko Â«Â ntaguhemukira ururimi rwacuÂ». Ngo bishitse bigakorwa mu zindi ndimi, umuntu ategerezwa kumenya neza ko uwo abihaye azi urwo rurimi. Ngo ariko birata akanovera, umuntu akabivuga nkâ€™uwikura, atamutima ubirimwoÂ ; ugapfa kurungika nkâ€™uko ubikuye kwa mugenzawe.
Kwipfurizanya ineza bivanye nâ€™umunezero, ni umugenzo mwiza mu barundi. Iyo umuntu ashikiwe nâ€™ineza, abamuri hafi bose barakorana bakamukeza. Eka nâ€™iyo bigenze ukundi agashikirwa nâ€™umubabaro, baramwegera bakamuremesha. Ivyo bigatuma umubano mwiza, ugufashanya, urukundo nâ€™amahoro bisasagara mu bantu.

Umuganuro Â nyezina
Hafi isaha ya gatanu yâ€™umusase, umurisho wâ€™ingoma waravumereye, uvuga ko ibirori bitanguye, umwami atanguye umuganuro. Nkâ€™ikiringo câ€™isaha nâ€™igice, abatimbo banonotse bidasanzwe barivuna barivunagura, imitima yâ€™abari aho iratwenga, iraremerana. Baragaragaje ubushobozi budasanzwe, bahiga imbere yacu natwe twatamariwe. Vyari ibirori koko.Â  Hakurikiye ikiyago câ€™abato nâ€™abakuze bibukanya ico ari co umuganuro. Baravuze ko â€œ Umuganuro wari ufise insiguro ikomeye, insiguro yâ€™ubumwe nâ€™akaranga biri mu bintu abakoroni bakuyeho kugira badutandukanye. ## Inyambo: inka yubahitse caneÂ kwâ€™isi
**Date:** November 29, 2017 2:40 pm  
**URL:** https://akanyaburunga.wordpress.com/2017/11/29/inyambo-inka-yubahitse-cane-kwisi/

Inyambo ni inka ihagurutse yari yubahitse cane mu Rwanda no mu Burundi bwâ€™aho hambere. Ni inka ifise ubwiza budasanzwe.Iyo nka ifise amahembe maremare, ateze neza cane ku buryo uyiravye usanga iberewe birenze urugero. Ifise mu maso hasenye neza nâ€™akanyabutatu ufatiye ku mahembe yayo. Iba iteze ishinze kandi igoroye. Iyo nka ikomoka kure cane kandi irubashwe hose.
Ishusho: commons.wikimedia.org
Ijambo â€œInyamboâ€ rirakoreshwa mu kirundi cane. Bararikoresha bariko baravuga ubwoko bwâ€™inka zakunda gutungwa mu mugamba canke iyo bariko baravuga ubwiza bwâ€™ikintu na canecaneÂ  ubwiza bwâ€™umukobwa. Musanzwe muzi ko umukobwa wâ€™umurundikazi bamugereranya nâ€™inka. Inyambo rero bivanye nâ€™ubwiza buyigaragarako bagaca barikoresha mu kugereranya umuntu wâ€™ubwiza bwinshi. Bavuze â€œgushaza manyamboâ€, bisigura kugenda neza nkâ€™inyambo ugendera ubwiza bwawe.
Vyâ€™inyamo, ziva ku gitungwa citwa reâ€™em mu giheburayo. Ico gitungwa kivugwa muri Bibiliya, incuro zishika icenda: Mu guharura (23,22) (24,8), Gusubira mu Vyagezwe (33,17), Yobu (39,9-10), Zaburi (22,21) (29,6) (92,11) na Izaya (34,7).
Izo nka zatanguye kuboneka mu ntara ya Rift Valey kuva muri Nubiya kumanuka gushika ku nkengera za Tanganyika. Zizwi ko zikomoka ku gisokuru cazo citwa â€œAurochsâ€, ikibogo kinini cazimanganye haraciye imyaka irenga ibihumbi umunani.Â  Bivugwa ko inka zakomotse kuri ico gisogokuru zagumye zimanuka zirisha mu ntara ya Lift Valey ariyo yitwa imbo igera ku nkengera za Tanganyika mu Burundi. Mu Rwanda no mu Burundi, izo nka zitwa inyambo, kuko zarangwa ku nkengera yâ€™uruzi Nili mu kiyaya câ€™imbo aho insazi Tse-Tse itashobora kuzirya. Â Mu bindi bihugu nko mu Buganda, izo nka bazita Ankole. Ahandi naho bazita Watusi kuko zatunzwe nâ€™aborozi bâ€™abatutsi baja baraziragira ku nkengera zâ€™uruzi. Nkâ€™uko vyandikwa nâ€™ishirahamwe mpuzamakungu yâ€™abatunganyambo (WWA), izo nka zahavuye zitwarwa mu budagi nâ€™ibindi bihugu vya Buraya, ziruhira kujanwa no muri Amerika aho zisigaye ari nyinshi (zirenga ibice 80%).
Zoba ziva mu ntara yâ€™imbo
Amahembe yazo ni maremare. Ishusho: commons.wikimedia.org
Bamwe bavuga ko zoba ziva mu ntara yâ€™imbo. Ngo abantu baba mu ntara za Mugamba nâ€™ahandi boba barabonye izonka zisangije uko zisa ziduganwa mu ntara zabo bagaca bazita iryo zina â€œInyamboâ€. I-nya-mbo. Iryo jambo ni izina ryâ€™urunani hagati yâ€™integuza I yongeweko indangakibanza nya nâ€™irindi jambo imbo. Bikumvikana ko izo nka ziva imbo.
Aba nyene bifashisha irindi zina ryâ€™inka nazo zitwa inyaruguru. Bavuga ko vyoba vyavuye ko ahatari imbo bakunda kuhita ruguru. Izo nka rero zikaba zakomoka ruguru. Bazihushanije rero nâ€™inyambo. Bikumvikana ko izikomoka mu ntara zindi zitwa inyaruguru izâ€™I mbo nazo zikitwa inyambo. Kandi ubwo bwoko bwâ€™inka buratandukanye biboneka. Inyaruguru ni inka zagutse, zifise igikuriro nâ€™amahembe matoya cane. Zitandukanye nâ€™inyambo. (Ankole)
Duhereye kuri ico ciyumviro canyuma, abandi bavuga ko atariyo kuko iyo bakuye amahembe yari inyambo igira amahembe maremare, iyo batayayikuye yari inyaruguru aguma ari magufi nyene.
Inka zubashwe cane
Mu Burundi no mu Rwanda, inyambo zari inka zâ€™ubwami. Inka zubashwe cane zama zivugirwa amazina bakazifata neza kuko nizo nka nyinshi wasanga umwami atunze. Kubera ubwiza bwazo, ubusho bwâ€™inka bwatungwa I Bwami bwaba ari ubwâ€™inyambo. Inka yâ€™inyambo bafata ko ari igitungwa gihezagiye. Â Inyambo ntiyapfa kubangurirwa impfizi iyo ariyo yose. Baraba nziza idoshe bakayiyibangurirako bagaca bayiha nâ€™umutobe kugirango ize ivyare iyo bisa, inyambo nkayo.
Mu Burundi, ubuzima bwose bwari bushingiye ku nka, kugeza aho hatereye urwimo. Inka yaza imbere yâ€™izindi nayo yari inyambo. Ico bubashe cose bacitirira ibiraba inka. Inda yâ€™umwami bayita â€œigisaboâ€, umugeni nawe bakamwita â€œinkaâ€, inka yâ€™amaguru abiri. Imbere yâ€™umuzo wâ€™abazungu, umuntu atunze inka niwe yari umutunzi wa mbere.
Mu bihe vya none, izo nka zirateye igomwe iyo uzibonye. Muri Amerika nâ€™I Buruaya, inka Watusi iratonye cane kuko bariko barazigwiza cane. Mu gihugu câ€™Urwanda hoho, Inyambo iri mu bintu vyinjiza amafaranga menshi mu bukerarugendo.

## Imigenzo iraba kurenga ibigo mu Burundi bwâ€™ahoÂ hambere
**Date:** October 17, 2017 10:11 am  
**URL:** https://akanyaburunga.wordpress.com/2017/10/17/imigenzo-iraba-kurenga-ibigo-mu-burundi-bw-aho-hambere/

Turamenyereye kwumva gutera intobo, gushinga icumu, gutahira nâ€™ibindi. Iyo yari imigenzo yeze mu miryango mu burundi bwâ€™aho hambere. No mu bihe vya none, usanga biriho nâ€™aho ubu bikorwa binyegejwe . Aho hambere hahise hoho vyari bifise ingene bikorwa, inzira wamengo yaranditswe ahantu nkâ€™uko mushobora kubisoma muri iki gisomwa.
Ishusho: commons.wikimedia
Mu myaka yacu, ibihe vyarahaye ibindi, imigenzo imwe iratituka iyindi iribagirwaÂ ; canke nyene irahindura ishusho. Kenshi rero kubera abarundi batandika, biratugora kumenya ivyakorwa aho hambere. Bitayeko ntivyanavugwa kenshi kuko murazi uburundi bugendera ku bizira. Hari rero ibintu bita ibiterasoni bitakunda kuvugirwa hejuru. Iyo bigiye biranyegezwa rero bica bigorana ukuntu biguma bitahurwa. Vyinshi muri ivyo , harimwo imigenzo ijanye noÂ  guhuza ibitsinaÂ : gutera intobo, gutahira, gushinga icumu, kwinjirira,nâ€™ibindi, yari igisibije.
Iyo migenzo yari ifise uko ikorwa womengo vyarumvikanyweko ku buryo uwo ari we wese abikurikiza uko. Yaba ubukora, yaba ubikorerwa ugasanga ni nkâ€™ibwirizwa ngenderwako rigenga iyo ngeso. Niho vyari vyaracitse umugenzo.
Gutera intobo
Abakurambere twaganiriye bambwiye ko uwo mugenzo wari ugwiriye mu Burundi. Mbere nâ€™ubu woba ukiba ahatari hake nâ€™aho boba batagikoresha intobo nkâ€™uko vyari kera.
Nkâ€™uko muvyumva muri iryo ryungikane, Â hakoreshwa Â«Â intoboÂ Â». Ni icamwaÂ  camurwa ku giti citwa umutobotobo gifise amahwa nâ€™amashami asanzarara. Bakunda ku bitera ku mihora canke ku nzitiro. Intobo uyimenye imbere harimwo utubutobuto nâ€™uburemborembo busa nâ€™umufyiri. Uyishize mu kanwa irarura igakata.
Mu gutera intobo, umugabo yararereka umukecuru wiwe ko yarenze irembo yaba agiye mu ndimiro canke kuvoma, agasoboka akaraba aho umukazana wiwe ariko arakubura canke ariko arakora utundi dukorwa twâ€™i muhira akajugunya ya ntobo imbere yiwe. Umukazana ayibonye yaba afise inyishu zibiri: yarayitora akayimusubiza. Muri ico gihe, umugabo yaca atahura ko umukazana amwankiye. Vyumvikana ko yoba ari mu butinyanka canke hari ikitamworohereza mu nzu. Umukazana ayanduye akayibika, maze akinjira mu nzu, sebukwe yarabona ko umukazana amubwiye ati â€œKaze nyakugira inka nâ€™ibibondo, uburiri nashashe , umunega nawe ari kure kandi vyose biratunganye ingo ngufate nezaâ€. Yaca yinjira akagenda bakarangura amabanga bagaheza agasubira agasohoka. Uko gufata neza rero ntikwari ugusigana amasoro, kuko bategerezwa kumakura nkâ€™abiba nyene.
Gutera intobo abakazana barabikunda kuko iyo bishitse bakibaruka umwana asa na sebukwe vyari bigoye kumwagiriza ko yarenze ibigo kuko yavuga ati ni ivyo nahawe nâ€™umugabo wanje. Vyari bitandukanye nâ€™aho yovyara abasa nâ€™umutwa yashora inkono hafi yâ€™iwabo, umwungere amuragirira inka canke uwundi badasangiye amaraso. Ikindi naco, ntiyatinya ivyo kuvyara icugane kuko yaba avuka ahandi, adasangiye amaraso na sebukwe. Ngo abana bavutse muri ubwo buryo barashobora kuba ari benshi cane.
Gushinga icumu
Ubu vyaragabanutse ariko aho hambere hahiseÂ  vyari bikaze cane. Vyakorwa kenshi nâ€™abatware kuko baba bazi ko bategerezwa kubatinya. Umugabo yaraza dogiridogiri no ku rugo rwawe ngo ba. Yaba yarahagendereje akamenya uko umugore wawe ameze canke yararungitse umutasi. Ashitse yararaba ko utahari. Akinjira. Asanze umugore wawe ashobora kumufata neza agaca ashinga icumu kwâ€™irembo akinjira mu nzu . Agakora icamuzanye.
Intangabutumwa ikomeye
Icumu rishinzwe kwâ€™irembo ryaba risigura ko hari uwundi mugabo yaritashe. Nyene urugo rero aje agasanga icumu rishinze, yaca ahinda ibogo akaja kuba arimanzamanza kugire agaruke wamazeÂ  kugenda. Carazira ntawinjirira ku mugabo yabonye icumu. Iyo yinjiye naho yaba agiye kumucumuta. Mugabo kuko atamenya ko uwuriyo ari umuganwa canke umwami, yahitamwo kugenda akagaruka hanyuma. Vyari bimaramaje kubona ukuviriye ku mugore!
MN: Ijambo umushingantahe rikomoka kuri uwu mugenzo. Umushingantahe yari umuntu yubashwa kuko yashinze icumu kwâ€™irembo iwawe utamwinjirirako.
Gutahira
Ibi navyo vyari bitandukanye nâ€™ivyo bibiri twumvise hejuru. Vyaba ku mugore ikibano cose kizi ko ari umupfakazi canke yahukanye. Yabuze umugabo akiri muto, yama aronka abatahira iminsi yose. Yamubuze akuze naho, ntiyababura ariko baba ari imparurwa.
Uwo mugore yama yiteguye iminsi yose kuko ntiyari azi igihe bamugendera. Ari muri vyabihe vyâ€™abapfasoni, baraza ariko akababwira ko bidasoboka. Yari afise uburyo bwo kubabwira ko atawe yakira.Â  Yamubwira ko â€œIkazanga ryâ€™amavuta yomusize ryagataye canke amavuta yacitseâ€, canke akaririmba kugire abana ntibamenye ico avuze.
Batahira baje kuryamana nâ€™uwo mugore. Uwo nawe ntiyateba gusama mu gihe atari ingumba. Umugabo yashengeye amusigiye abana, abo yaca abakurikiza abo akuye ku bagabo batahira. Ivyo vyatuma usanga umugore aguma yibaruka kandi yarabuze umugabo canke barahukanye.
Kenshi uwatahiye yaca asiga ateye ikintu nkâ€™umugano, umurinzi, canke ikindi giti gikura cane kugire yerekane ko yahaciye. Ico giti carakura kigakurana nâ€™umwana. Ari ingundu yâ€™umugano yaca iba iyo bazomusohoza akuze kuko nâ€™aho bamugora ngo ntatorane kuko yavyawe nâ€™uwundi, ico caba ikimenyetso câ€™uko afise ico ahagaba.
Ingorane yo gutahira yari ubwambere na mbere ku bana. Baba ari bato canke bakuze, baguma babona iwabo urunkweknwe rwâ€™abagabo nâ€™imiburiburi nkâ€™iminsi icumi mu kwezi. Muri abo baba bazi ko ata se arimwo canke haje se wâ€™umwe canke uwâ€™uwundi.
Iyo migenzo yose yerekana ukuntu ukurenga ibigo kwari kwariraye mu barundi bâ€™aho hambere. Hari aho vyafatwa nkâ€™ubutore, ubugabo canke ubundi buhizi, ariko vyama vyakweze inzankano, insaku, ukwinubana ndetse nâ€™ingwara nyinshi. Nâ€™aho umugera wa ruhonyanganda utari bwaze, baranduzanya ibindi bitari bike.

## Menya akahise kawe:  Kumenja nkaÂ Barera
**Date:** April 16, 2017 3:37 pm  
**URL:** https://akanyaburunga.wordpress.com/2017/04/16/menya-akahise-kawe-kumenja-nka-barera/

Izina â€œBareraâ€ rirakunda gokoreshwa mu kirundi ryongewe ku yandi majambo rikaba iryungikane. Ivyo bituma umuntu yibaza vyinshi kuri iryo zina nâ€™ayo majambo arikomokako. Akibaza nimba Barera yari umuntu, nâ€™ivyamuranze bigatuma avugwa nkâ€™uko.
Ishusho: Youtube
Izina Barera abaroranya imvugo na kahise bohava barishira ku ntwaro ya gikoroni aho abazungu baza gucura bufuni na buhoro Afirika yari yiganziwe nâ€™ubwami butandukanye nâ€™ingoma yâ€™Uburundi irimwo. Aho boba bafatiye ku mvugo yâ€™iryo zina yegeranye na ca gisagara câ€™Ubudagi caberamwo inama yâ€™amagaburabutaka yo 1885. Ico gisagara citwa Berile; umuntu yokwibaza ko arico nkomoko yâ€™irya jambo Barera na canecane ko ariho havuye akabi kose karuhije basogokuru. Canakwira nâ€™abadagi nibo baciye biyizira gucunaguza abarundi; kandi kanatsinda nâ€™iryo zina Barera rikunze kwungikanywa nâ€™amabi gusa.
Ihibambewe, mu matohoza twagize twasanze Barera yari umuntu kandi ataho ahuriye nâ€™ubukoroni kuko yari umurundi. Abatohozi bâ€™imico nâ€™imigenzo na Kahise twabajije batubwiye ko Barera yari umuntu atonye cane I bwami.
Ingoma yâ€™umukazo udasanzwe
Ngo hari ku ngoma yâ€™umwami Mwambutsa III Mbonuburundi batazira Nyamubi (1732-1740). Iryo zina ryâ€™iritazirano yarihawe kubera ukuntu yagisibije mu co yaramutswa. Yarangaje abantu, abandi arabanyaga eka mbere nâ€™abaganwa aragarika.Â  Abakera baremeza ko ingoma yiwe yararemereye abarundi bidasanzwe.
Turamaze kwumva ko Abambutsa bari bamenyereye kutiha ubuki nkâ€™abandi bami, nkâ€™abatare nâ€™abezi hamwe nâ€™abataga.Â  Abambutsa bose bahereza kwambuka bakaja gusazira kure yâ€™ubwami. Mwambutsa Nyamubi rero yipfuje kudeha iryo ragi agomba gusaza aganza mu Burundi kandi atihaye ubuki. Umuntu wese rero yabona yomumerera nabi yaca amwica; nâ€™abana biwe ntiyabagera umutwe na rirya aribo bari kuvamwo abamukura ku ngoma. Abahungu bavuka yaca abica. Ivyo ntivyanezera abarundi kuko babona ariko ararenga indahiro. Abahanuzi baramuhanura akica amatwi.
Ishavu ryâ€™abanyagihugu
Wawundi ati igihugu si icana. Abarundi barabonye ko umwami yananiranye. Baciye biga umugambi wo kumugondoza. Baremeye barakora ibizira, barenga iryo Imana yâ€™abarundi yari yarabategetse kuva Uburundi bukibaho.
Kuva kera ishamba rya kibira ryari iryâ€™Imana. Umwami Mwezi Gisabo yari yarasubiye arabishimikako, aributsa ko ishamba rya Kibira rihuza isi nâ€™ijuru, Imana nâ€™abantu. Yaguma yihaniza abantu ngo ntibahirahire ngo baje kugicamwo ibiti.Â  Ivyo vyari ivyo kuva kera cane.
Abanyagihugu rero babonye Mwambutsa yimonogoje baca barengera mu kibira baragihumbira kugira ngo Imana ipfume ishavura isuke ishavu ryayo ku mwami kuko yari yaganguye.Â  Bavuga ko igihugu caciye kimererwa nabi, haratera isibe. Abahanuzi baciye baremera umwami ngo yihe ubuki ku nguvu.
Barera, umuhanuzi wâ€™umuhemu
Aremerewe nâ€™abashingantahe, abahanuzi nâ€™abanyamabanga, umwami yaremeye kwiha ubuki mbere, nkâ€™uko vyari bitegetswe ku mwami wese yamenye ibanga, baca bamuturirana nâ€™ingoro arimwo. Ikirimba kigasiba ntihagire nâ€™uwuzosubira kuhaja.
Mu bahanuzi bagumye bosha nabi umwami harimwo uwitwa Barera. Uwo yaguma amwemerera ko ivyo azokora vyose azomugwa inyuma. Ngo yari umwosha mubi gushika no ku munsi wa nyuma wâ€™ubuzima bwâ€™umwami.
Barera rero yategerezwa kwereka umwami ko amuguye inyuma. Afata umukenke kumwe nâ€™umwami, ariko aho gukwega ubuki agumizamwo umukenke gusa. Ahengera umwami aracikanye, aca asohoka yiruka atungwa nâ€™ayo yameze.
Abantu nabo bari bakinje bakikuje ikirimba ivyo vyariko biberamwo. Bari bagabirije kugire bace bakonga ingoro bayiturije imyampi yaka imbeya. Bagize bartya babona Barera asohotse yiruka baca bamuhurizako ya myampi abandi amacumu. Aguma yiruka avirirana baramukurikira. Baramufata bamukubita buyoka nkâ€™umumenja nyene. Aca apfa nabi.
Kuva ico gihe, umuntu wâ€™umunyamayeri canke wâ€™ikibi bamwita Barera. Umuntu arinda cane nkâ€™umwihevyi bakamwita iryo zina. Hari nâ€™amungikane menshi akoresha iryo zina nka: kurinda nka Barera, kugoka nka Barera, kumenja nka Barera,â€¦

## Menya akahise kawe : 8Â Ntwarante
**Date:** March 8, 2017 3:04 pm  
**URL:** https://akanyaburunga.wordpress.com/2017/03/08/menya-akahise-kawe_8_ntwarante/

Benshi bakunze kuvuga ko uwa 8 Ntwarante ari umunsi mpuzamakungu wahariwe abakenyezi. Abandi nabo bumva ko ahubwo woba wahariwe agateka kiwe. Kugira dutahure ico arico, twashimye kubaza kahise kâ€™uwo munsi udasanzwe.
Ishusho:africatimes
Uwo munsi waje inyuma yâ€™ukwitanga kwinshi, uburuhe nâ€™umunangiro wo gusaba uburenganzira bwo gutora, kworoherezwa mu kazi hamwe nâ€™inganishwa ryâ€™umukenyezi nâ€™umugabo. Iyo ntambara yaranyiganyije cane uburaya nâ€™ibihugu vyâ€™uburengero bwâ€™isi mu ntango yâ€™ikinjana ca mirongo ibiri.
Kopenehage muri Danemarike
Umunsi mpuzamakungu wahariwe abakenyezi wavuzwe ubwa mbere mu mwaka wâ€™1910, mu nama mpuzamakungu igira kabiri yâ€™abakenyezi nkomezamibano. Wavuzwe nâ€™umudagikazi wâ€™umumenyeshamakuru Karara Zethkin.
Hari i Kopenehage muri Danemarike, muri Myandagaro 1910, mu nama ya kabiri yahuje abakenyezi amajana nâ€™amajana bari baje baturuka mu bihugu 17 bitandukanye kwâ€™isi.Â  Inama yambere yaheruka kuba mu mwaka 1907 ku ciyumviro ca wa mumenyenshamakurukazi ico gihe yari arongoye ikinyamakuru Die Gleichheit (Ukungana)Â  Ikinyamakuru cakundwa cane, ico gihe cari gifise abasomyi barenga 125 000.
Muri iyo nama, niho uwo mukenyezi Karara Zethkin yasaba, ku ncuro yambere, ko abakenyezi nkomezamibano bo kwâ€™isi yose boshinga umunsi wahariwe abakenyezi uko umwaka utashe. Kwari kugire uzobabere nkâ€™intango yo kugwanira uburengenzira bwo gutora ku bagore. Ico ciyumviro nticatevye kwemezwa. Intumbero ya masha yâ€™uwo munsi, yari iyo kuronka uburengenzira bwo gutora, kuko nta mukenyezi yari abirekuriwe.Uwo munsi nta genekerezo kanuni bavuyeho bashinze.
Mu mwaka wakurikiye, igenekerezo rya 19 Ntwarante 1911, niho abakenyezi bababa umuliyoni bihereza amabarabara mu bihugu bitari bike vyâ€™I Bulaya no muri Leta zunze ubumwe za Amerika. Ivyo vyari Ubudagi, Ubusuwisi, Otirishe hamwe na Danemarike. I Beriline mu Budagi, amahuriro 45 yahuje abakenyezi barenga 40 000. I Vyene muri Otirishe, abakenyezi barenga 30 000 bihereje amabarabara bahimbaza umunsi wabahariwe.
Aho hose baguma basaba iyubahirizwa ryâ€™agateka kabo. Hejuru yâ€™uburenganzira bwo gutora nâ€™uburenganzira bwo kuja mu mabanga yâ€™igihugu, abo akenyezi basaba kurekurirwa kuja mu buzi bwa leta nâ€™ikurwaho ryâ€™ubusumbasumbane mu kazi bwari bwarimonogoje. Aho hose igenekerezo nyene izina ntiryari bwashingwe ku mugaragaro.
Italiki ya 8 ntwarante yatanguye gufatwa nkâ€™umunsi mpuzamakungu wâ€™abakenyezi mu 1917. Vyatanguriye kuri yegere yegere yâ€™abakenyezi aho bihereje amabarabara basaba imfungurwa nâ€™abagabo babo bari barungitswe ku rugamba. Hari mu gisagara citiriwe Umweranda Peteroburugu, umugwa mukuru wâ€™uburusiya wâ€™ico gihe. Hari kwâ€™igenekerezo rya 23 Ruhuhuma ku kiranga minsi ca Geregori, bihurirana nâ€™igenekerezo rya 8 Ntwarante ku kirangaminsi ca Yuriyano dukoresha ubu.
Kuva uwo mwaka, uwa 8 Ntwarante, wagumye ari umunsi mpuzamakungu wahariwe umukenyezi nâ€™agateka kiwe . Inyuma yâ€™Â 1945, uwo munsi waciye utangura guhimbazwa kwâ€™isi yose.
Ukwiyubura kwâ€™uwo munsi
Uwo munsi wagiye kwiyongera inguvu mu myaka yâ€™imvyurabukenyezi ya 70.Â  Uwo munsi wemewe nâ€™ishirahamwe mpuzamakungu mu 1977. Mu bufaransa naho wemewe ku mugaragaro 1982. Mu Burundi, ako gateka abakenyezi bakaronse kuva kera. Amatora agitanguzwa mu gihugu kuwa 18 Nyakanga1961, abakenyezi baratoye banashikana umugambwe wâ€™abadasigana ku ntsinzi itazibagirwa, yatumye igihugu cikukira.
Uwa 8 ntwarante, si umunsi mpuzamakungu wahariwe abakenyezi. Iminsi yose ni iyabo. Ahubwo iryo genekerezo, ryahariwe kwibukiriza agateka kâ€™umukenyezi nâ€™intambwe amaze gutera kuva muri kahise.

**Date:** July 18, 2024 5:30 pm

Harabaye umugabo arongora umugoreê“¹ uwo mugore aribugenga, ageze kwibaruka, ngâ€™uyo akize gushikana gusa aca arapfa. Umwana asigaye ku ngoyi bamwita Kabindiê“¹ umugabo wiwe aca yiyumvira kurongora uwundi kuko yari akiri mutoê“¹ yibwira ko uno azomufasha kurera umwana yasigaye ku ngoyi.

Ntivyatevye ku mugoroba wa mugore artahaê“¹ umugabo na we akirindiriye ko inka zitaha, niko guheza akabaza akaze cane uwamenye umubindi, vyakabaye kera MunwaÂ  acaramena ibanga aravuga ko Kabindi ariwe yawumenye. Nâ€™ishavu nâ€™akantuê“¹ wa mugore arengera kuri Kabindi aramukubita gushika amwisheê“¹ aca aramuburuta mushikana ahantu hari intore musi yâ€™urugo amuhambaho. Umugabo atashe arabaza iyo umwana wiwe ari, maze umukobwa na nyina bararahira bararengwa ko batazi iyo yagiye. Iminsi irahera baragenda kurondera kwa nyina bo, sekuru, inasenge eka Â mwâ€™ibenga barabura.
Vyaratevye Munwa aja kuvoma, hageze ko yiremeka aca aterera mwâ€™ijwi agira ati :
â€œKubura kene wacu kaza kundemeka x 2â€œ. Aca yumva akajwi kamusubiza kagira kati:
â€œAkarimi koba ako (x 2), hamwe wandega kwa mama, ukandegandega (x 2) bakantematema (x 2) bakanta mu ntore, imvura ynya mukuku ikankukumura, Imana nyamwengenga iranyengenga intwara mwâ€™ibenga, akarimi koba ako â€œx 2)â€œ.
Wa mwana nâ€™ubwoba nâ€™akantu aterera wa mubindi hasi agenda ariruka no muhira ahasanga se araheza amwiganira ko yumvise ijwi rya mukuru we igihe yari kuvoma. Se bimutera amakenga aca amubwira ko bojana akamwereka aho yamwumvise, wa mwana aja imbere, se arakurikira baragenda gushika ku mwonga , se aca yinyegeza inyuma yâ€™agasaka, Munwa atangura guterera mu gahogo kumwe kwa mbere agira ati: â€œKubura kubura kene wacu kaza kundemeka x 2â€œ. Yongera kwumva akajwi kamusubiza kagira kati:
â€œAkarimi koba ako (x 2), hamwe wandega kwa mama, ukandegandega (x 2) bakantematema (x 2) bakanta mu ntore, imvura ynya mukuku ikankukumura, Imana nyamwengenga iranyengenga intwara mwâ€™ibenga, akarimi koba ako â€œx 2)â€.
Se ahejeje kwumva uko vyagenze aca arataha ishavu riniga asanga mugore wiwe ariko aracumba ahitana ubuhiri abumukubita mu mutwe acaracikana ubwo nyene.
Si je nohahera, hohera uwo mugore yapfuye azira ubukozi bwâ€™ikibi.

â€“ Egome.

â€“ Navuze ko Imana ariyo nkuru, ari yo igaba abantu, yo irema.

â€“ Si uko wavuze?

â€“ Igumire aho.
â€“ Nawe wa gisizimwe we, ntuvuze ko Imana ari yo nkuru, ari yo igaba abantu, yo irema?
â€“ Egome.

â€“ Urwanje ntiruhera nâ€™ejo nzinduka ngenda.

Inarunyonga ni umugore yakora ivyo abandi badakora. Yambara nkâ€™abagabo ata mugore nâ€™umwe wo mu gihe ciwe yovyubahuka, agakora ico cose kitorohera abandi bagore. Tumusanga mu bujajuro, eka nâ€™imigani myinshi arayivugwamwo. Nkâ€™uyu uvuga ukuntu yabeshe umwami. Soma musoserwe!
Ishusho: Commons.wikimedia
Umusi umwe, umwami yabajije Runyonga ateramiye ku kirimba aho yari yashengeye mu bandi bagabo ati: â€œMbegaÂ  Runyonga, numvise ngo nyoko arahendana, ni vyo? â€
Uri uwundi ati: â€œMwami wâ€™i Burundi, ntibabesha na mba. Nawe yoguhenda!â€
Nâ€™agasuzuguro kenshi umwami aritwengera. Azunza umutwe gatatu imbere yo kumwamirira kure avuga ati: â€œOya sinohendwa nâ€™umugore nawenu. Uramuzana agerageze turabeâ€.

## Ese urubutiro!
**Date:** October 11, 2017 9:19 am  
**URL:** https://akanyaburunga.wordpress.com/2017/10/11/ese-urubutiro/

Urubutiro rwâ€™umutima nâ€™urwo ku mubiri! Turi muri vyabikorwa nyene. Hakoreshejwe ya majambo nyene inkwano, urutaro, urubutiro, igisamamajonjo, gucererwa, urume, ku wâ€™Imana, Porosuperi Niyonkuru aduha impanuro zidasanzwe, Gerevasi nawe akaduha inkuru ibabaje cane. Bose bahuriye ko batubwira ibijanye nâ€™urubutiro. Ibi vyose vyanditswe mu minota itanu. Soma usoserwe.
Ishusho: pixabay
Tugire amahoro!
Mbega harya ugucerwa biremewe? Kuwâ€™Imana uja ubona umuntu arinamuye, ikaruvati mwâ€™izosi, ikirato gisongoye nkâ€™umusumari canke yabwegereje imvutano nohejuru yâ€™abantu bariko barazirikana ngo dododo. Wobeshera igisamamajonjo hejuru yâ€™intama, ubona ko kidakomwakomwa.
Â 
Uje gusenga, utegerezwa kuzinduka, Â ukigaba. Bitagenze uko naho, ubonye ugiye gucerwa, uziterera ku rutugu ukayakoramwo. Ukiruka bwiruke nâ€™ikaruvati mwâ€™izosi kandi naho yokoroka ntunobe kugirango ushike kugihe. Vyanse ko wiruka ukagira ku rutaro kugira ngo ntihagire ugutanga imigisha yambere. Ivyo vyose rero ga, ukabikora mu mwanya urume rumara, kugira ntusange umukozi wâ€™Imana yamaze gutanga ikigongwe ubona ko wama wiyanduje nkâ€™ingurube yiyanduza iri munzu. Kuko usanze yamaze kugitanga, woba usa nâ€™umuvyeyi ariye urubutiro.
Mwavyumvise ga basha?
Porosuperi Niyonkuru arangije Kaminuza yâ€™Uburundi mu gisata câ€™Imbagarabwonko. Asanzwe ari mu banditsi ba Yaga

Â 
Umuvyeyi yariye urubutiro
Â 
Umutama
Ku wâ€™Imana uheze nari ngiye gusenga. Naciye mu muhana uri hafi yâ€™iwacu ndabashiriye urutaro twari twabatijije. Nasanze umugore waho yarariye urubutiro mbabazwa nâ€™ukuntu uwo muvyeyiÂ  yakowe inkwano zâ€™umurengera akabura ico kumuhembura. Nâ€™umubabaro mwinshi narabandanije urugendo.

Nari nazindutse cane nibwira ko ntaja gucerwa ariko ngize nrtya mbona igisamamajonjo cagaye mu nzira kintera ubwoba nsubira inyuma nirika.Â  Ariko rero ndavye mbona nticankurikiye nca nsubira kubandanya ndacegera. Gica kiguma kigendera imbere yanje. Natomboreyemwo kuko nasanze kigenda kirankumira urume.

## Umugani: Rutwe aja gusabaÂ umugeni
**Date:** October 9, 2017 9:26 am  
**URL:** https://akanyaburunga.wordpress.com/2017/10/09/umugani-rutwe-aja-gusaba-umugeni/

Amajambo twahanye twisunga yari:Â inkwano, urutaro, urubutiro, igisamamajonjo, gucererwa, urume, ku wâ€™Imana. Soma igisomwa cavuyemwo. Tugikesha mugenzi wacu Nsengiyumva Benedigito.

Harabaye umusore akitwa Rutwe rwa Ndanibenga. Yarabaye ngaho ataco yibwira kugira ngo yubake urwiwe nkâ€™abandi basore, maze abantu bakaguma bamuryanira inzara kubera yazinduka ku kirabo gushengerera aho babaga. Haciye iminsi babahimiriza, agatumba kabako Rutwe kose karagiye kwigira urubatizo. Abato, abakuze, bose baragenda. Nawe Rutwe ararahira aranana ko atazohonyorayo. Yigumira ari umuzira rumenyetso. Yibwira ko ugiye gusenga udasubira kuronka uruhusha rwo kuja aratuneza ubuhiye. Ariko uko iminsi yahera, bagenzibe bagumye bamukwegakwega.
Umunsi umwe yaritoye aja gusenga ku wâ€™Imana nkâ€™abandi, niho yabona umukobwa ateye igomwe ashogomanze yitahiye, Rutwe rwa Ndanibenga igitima ngo kwa! Atangura kumukurikira ku runo ku runo. Umukobwa ahindukiye ukamengo kwa Rutwe ijuru rirururutse. Niko kwibwira ati reka nanje ndarivuge aho vyakabereye ni kera. Ca gihwa kiniga abahungu batamenyereye kuresha kiramuhagama ariko uwo munsi Rutwe yari yamaze kurya karungu. Ni uko rero acakira ya nkumi ya barundi arayigumya ukuboko, ntiyibutse no kumuramutsa ayibwira ati, Â«Â ndagukunda, kandi nshaka ko twubakanaÂ !Â Â» Umukobwa nawe ntiyari agifise iryo asubizayo kubera yabona Rutwe icuya gica irya nâ€™ino. Umutima wiwe watera indihaguzi, wari kugira ngo ni umuvuba bariko baravuguta. Inyuma yâ€™agacerere katari gato niho wa mwigeme yikurayo ati, Â«Â Ukaba unkunda uraze ubisabe abavyeyi banje, unyereke vyâ€™ukuri ko uri umuhungu wâ€™ijambo.Â Â»
Rutwe yavuye ngaho yiruka agenda aratamba atarika, ashitse muhira abwira umuryango ko yarirashe rikagema. Ni uko rero baranezerwa bategura amashishiro nâ€™ibisabisho bazotwara gusaba umugeni. Bukeye mu gatondo bazindutse barahunja urume banyaragasa kugira ngo ntibacererwe abo iwabo naÂ  wa mukobwa bahave baronka umwanya wo gukora amatohoza ku nyifato ya Rutwe.
Bamaze gushikayo basanga iwabo wâ€™umukobwa bamaze kwitegura, bararura imfungurwa zo kwakira umukwe, bazana nâ€™inzoga zengetse baratereka. Rutwe ngo abibone amate atangura kwuzura akanwa, aho yicaye atangura gusutwasutwa. Serugo rero atangura araramutsa amahoro, ashikiriza ijambo ryo kwakira abashitsi yongera ababaza nâ€™ikibagenza, abaherekeje umuhungu barashikiriza iryabazinduye nawe nyene urugo arateba arabemerera ko azobagabira nkuko babisavye. Inyuma yâ€™aho abahereza imfungurwa nâ€™ibinyobwa barihereza. Wa muhungu Rutwe nawe abirengerako arabiromagira nkâ€™igisamamajonjo, icibo kingana nâ€™urutaro agisiga ceraÂ ; abari ngaho barumirwa. Bene umukobwa ngo babibone gurtyo bibwira bati, Â«Â uwo muntu arya nkâ€™isiha nta mugeni wacu tumuha yohava amurira munzu, canke akamurisha urubutiro.Â Â»
Ni uko barikebukanya bakira inkwano zose na za nzoga bamwana yari yarungitse bazikoreza abikorezi bababwira bati gende muronderere ahandi umugeni wacu turacamukeneye. Rutwe mwene Ndanibenga aba abuze umugeni kubera amarara yiwe.
Sije nohahera hohera uwo muhungu wâ€™inda ndende yabuze umugeni kubera ubukunzi bwâ€™inda.

Kworora vyari vayarabaciyeÂ  inyuma.Â  Bari baragerageje kwiyamvya ngo batunge inka birababana urwÃªma. Impene biba uko. Intama biba uko, Inkwavu zo zapfa bataranazishikana mu kirutu. Inkoko zo ntiyari kwiyamvya ubuca ntibwari kumukundira ko atunga nâ€™ibaba na rimwe. Ababanyi ntibasiba kumuha ayera ngo aragowe nta nâ€™imbeba atunze kuko atacura nâ€™igihori.
Ariko rero, Imana yari yaramuhezagiye imuha amaboko meza. Yararima akimbura. Nâ€™aho yari yaragwijije abana barya ibiteye itongo, ntibabimara. Inzara yarabaza. Abandi batwa bama batonze kwa wa mugabo baje gusega canke basaba igikebere. Hari nâ€™abahutu, eka mbere nâ€™abatutsi yama asabisha.
Ntibitevye, umwaka umwe isibe riratera vyose birayoka. Abantu bose bagwa mu bukene budasanzwe na wa mutwa adasigaye inyuma. Ico gihe, kugire umuryango ushobore gukora ku munwa, yari intambara.
Umutwa rero wewe yari yarimbuye ibitari bike bimwe mu bigega, ibindi mu bitiba ibindi ku rusika. Hari nâ€™ivyo yari yarahomeye mu nzavya. Aho isibe ritereye rero uwo mutwa ntiyigeze agira ingorane zo kubaho kuko yari afise vyinshi.
Amezi nâ€™amezi abantu bahwera na kigoyi; umutwa nâ€™abâ€™iwe nabo bari mu gahimbo katagira izina. Umutwa ntiyasiba kwirata kubo bahuye bose avuga ko ari agahambaye.
Umunsi uri izina aja kuraba umuntu yigeze kumusabisha nawe akiri umusore yari ku mutumba ugira gatatu uvuye aho uwo mutwa yaba. Aho yaca hose yagenda arabona imihindigiti yâ€™abantu bayamitswe na kigoyi akenyo akararika. We yabona ngo abo bariko barishura ibicumuro bakoze. Ashitse kwa wa mugabo amusanga yigonye mu ntaba za ruguru abana bamwizinze iruhande. Arashika araramutsa baramwakira.
â€œUri aho ga wangabiye!â€, wa mutwa araramutsa.
â€œUri aho ga wangamburukiye!â€, uri uwundi aramwishura.
Nâ€™agahemo kenshi gacanze agatsengeneke, umutwa aratwenga wa mugabo ariko biherera mu ntamatama. Inyundo irakura ntisumvya iyayujuje. Iteka ryari rikiri kuri wa mugabo. Atari ukumugirira ikigongwe umutwa ntiyari kwubahuka ngo amucire inyeri nkâ€™uko abigirira abandi.
Baraganira baranavuga ku kiza camaze abantu. Aho umutwa we yacira agati mu ryinyo yibwira ngo bizohora ukwo.
Yasubiye inyuma yagaye nkâ€™igikere umengo asumba isi nâ€™ijuru bikoranye. Yagenda aradembwa ahana nâ€™imbwa imihindigito yasanga yiyanikiye ku zuba kubera kigoyi.
Ntibukeye kabiri, umutwa abona abana biwe nâ€™umugore bagenda barahibagira abandi babanyi bagenda ku ruti rwâ€™umugongo. Wawundi ati itunga rirasaza. Bugorovye, umutwakazi yahakuye icibo cuzuye umutsima wâ€™uburo azana ikindi barakoza, bararya barahimba; baradurarara.Â  Umutwa utanka, inyuma yo gushika ku buriri aho aryama bimugoye, yategetse umutwakazi ko yoturira ca kigega nâ€™ibitiba ngo ntavyuke abisangaho kuko yahaze ntavyo agikeneye. Umutwakazi kuko yari azi ko yinjiranye inkazi aca aramwumvira arabikonga vyose ariko yabanje kubidaha akonga ibisasa gusa.Â  Aca arara arabijana iwabo afashijwe nâ€™abana bose.
Bukeye umugabo aravyuka, yanda yahotse yumva itanguye kumuharamba. Ahamagara umugore wiwe Â ngo amucumbire ubwo yizinduza aramubura, umwana mukuru arabura, uwukurikira biba uko nyene. Â Umutwa aca asigara yigonye aho nyene atagira nâ€™ico ashira ku munwa vyose babitwayeÂ ; umugore nâ€™abana nabo baca bibera kwa sekuru bafise ivyo barya.
Haheze iminsi wa mutwa, kubera atari yaramenyereye gutubika umukanda, aca atangura kugwara umugatu, ikigoyi gica kiramugatura. Haheze iminsi ibiri abwanuye, imvura yari yataze ica iragwa, amatongo asubira kumera aratotahara.

## #Icuramayagwa: imigenzo mibi, ivyamwaÂ bibi
**Date:** September 25, 2017 3:56 pm  
**URL:** https://akanyaburunga.wordpress.com/2017/09/25/icuramayagwa-imigenzo-mibi-ivyamwa-bibi/

Indongorabiyago yo kuri uwu wa gatatu igenekerezo rya 20 Nyakanga 2017 yavuga iti: â€œAmase ya kera atagihoma urutaro: Imizi yâ€™imico ndemakabi mu migenzo yâ€™ikirundiâ€. Â Yararyoheye abari bahashitse bose. Barahanahanye ivyiyumviro bidasanzwe ku bijanye nâ€™imigenzo mibi nkâ€™uko twabiyagiwe nâ€™uwari arongoye ico kiyago. Nâ€™aho we yari yateguye imizi yâ€™imigenzo mibi gusa, vyaranse ko boganda badaciye ku mayange imigenzo myiza iranga abarundi. Kurikira.
Ishusho: Prosper N.
Uwatuyagira, umusore Nisenti Irambona, yaratwiganiye vyinshi ku migenzo mibi iguma iranga abarundi iyo baja hose. Yahereye ku mugenzo mubi wo gucerwa. Ntawobideha, ico kibi kibishe kiravugwa ku barundi bose. Iyo umuntu ashitse ku masaha , benshi baratangara bakavuga ngo â€œsha, nyamba uri umuzungu. Ko uzindinduka cane!â€ Nkâ€™uko umengo umurundi ntavyo yoshobora. Benshi baramaze kumugara. Niho uja wumva ngo amasaha yâ€™abarundi, nâ€™ibindi vya ndagutakiye bigaragaza ko abarundi batubahiriza isaha na gato. Nta nkeka ko babibesha ariko vyaramaze kuba bwome.
Ikiyago cabandanirije ku mwibutsa: umuryambwa aba umwe agatukisha umuryango, umwibutsa werekana ko umuntu akwiye kwitwara neza azi neza ko akoze nabi aba agomba gucafuza abandi, nkâ€™uko wumva twese abarundi tuzwi ngo turacerwa kandi atari twese.
Ikindi caje kitoroshe cabaye ikibazo câ€™ubusuma. Nisenti yaravuze vyinshi atarya umunwa, mbere yemeza ko nâ€™umugenzo wo kunyonyeza itunga ryâ€™igihugu ufise imizi mibi mu mugenzo wo kwiba wagumye uranga abarundi. Aho yaguma atanga uturorero mu mayagwa yâ€™aho hambere nkâ€™igisomwa â€˜Ni ntakwiba nzoguha inkaâ€™ benshi bazi mu mashure matoya; Imyibutsa ngo Umugabo ni uwurya utwiwe nâ€™utwâ€™abandi , uwutabenshe ntasumira umana,â€¦ Uwo mugenzo aho hambere wari ubuhizi.
Hari inyifato mbi bateye ivyatsi ishobora kuba yavuye kuri iyo migenzo mibi nkâ€™ubwicanyi, ubusambanyi, ukurenga amategeko nâ€™ibigirankana,â€¦
Imigenzo myiza yovomererwa
Nâ€™ubwo ari uko, mu Burundi hari imigenzo myiza myinshi ikwiye kuvomerwa nkâ€™uko benshi babivuze. Aha uwitwa Etienne yaradondaguye myinshi harimwo ugufashanya, twumva mu mwibutsa ngo nyamwigendako ntarimira impeshi; kugendera ukuri, twumva mu mwibutsa ngo ukuri guca mu ziko ntigusha. We asaba ko twogerageza kugendera vyiza tukabisasagaza, bibi navyo tukabigwanya twivuye inyuma.
Canakwira Uburundi bwa nyaburunga ntibwari buzwi ku bwicanyi. Ahubwo bwamye buzwi ku bantu bâ€™ubuhizi, bakunda igihugu, babana neza, abashingantahe bagendera ingingo nâ€™ijambo hamwe nâ€™abapfasoni bafise urupfasoni rudasanzwe.
Igihugu bavuze ko ari icâ€™amata nâ€™ubuki ntivyava ku busa. Barabona ko koko gitemba amahoro nâ€™amahonda.
Akamaro kâ€™icuramayagwa
Abari aho baremeje bose ko atayindi nzira yo gukomeza ivyiza, kubivomera, kuvumagura akabi no kukarandurana nâ€™imizi atari icuramayagwa. Â Amayagwa arafasha mwâ€™iterambere ryâ€™imibano. Arafasha kwumva ikitari umugenzo mwiza mbere akanafasha guteza imbere imigenzo ibereye. Nta nkeka ko ariyo nzira irama izodutuma twibuka ko ibanga riheberwa, ubuntu bukihabwa nawo umubano mwiza ukagwiza amasabo.
Munyuma, Â nkâ€™uko vyama, twakoze umwimenyerezo wo kwandika amayagwa waryoheye abantu cane. Abatari bwawubone baratangaye cane babonye mu minota itarenga itanu bashobora kwandika inkuru iryoshe kandi iryohoye ifise intango nâ€™iherezo.
#Icuramayagwa
Ku ncuro ya kane urwaruka rwarahuye ruganira ku kamaro kâ€™incuramayagwa mu guhindura imigenzo. pic.twitter.com/YTQsoerRxY
â€” Niyonizigiye Rivardo (@mbanyariva) 25 September 2017
Twarangirije kuri kagakino, agapfindo: Umunota wâ€™Ikirundi.
Ni aho ubutaha!

Nâ€™ubu mu manza zimwezimwe niko bimeze.

## Imyibutsa irora kuÂ Mana
**Date:** February 15, 2016 10:49 am

Vyegeranijwe na BÃ©noÃ®t Nsengiyumva
Hari benshi biyumvira ko kwemera no gusenga Imana vyoba vyazanywe nâ€™abazungu kuva aho haziye amadini atandandukanye yaba aya Gikirisu canke ayandi. Ihibambe we! Kuva kera na rindi abarundi baremera Imana mbere bakayitazira amazina atandukanye: Rugiravyose , Mushoboravyose, Mugabavyose, Rurema, nâ€™ayandi nâ€™ayandi. Uretse nivyo abarundi barisunga ubushobozi bwâ€™Imana mukwita amazina abana, muguca imigani, mukurahira, mu myibutsa, no mubuzima busanzwe bwa misi yose.
Abanywanyi bâ€™akanyaburunga wa murwi uhora ubayagira ibijanye nâ€™akaranga kuri Makuruki nâ€™ ikinyamashusho washimye kugaruka kumyibutsa ndoramana abarundi bakunda gukoresha kera. Iyo nayo irerekana neza ingene Imana yamye iri imbere mu mico yacu. Nkuko mushobora kuyitahura iyi myibutsa yerekana ingene abarundi baha ikibanza ca mbere Imana. Kera baraja mubapfumu, bagaterekera, ariko uravye imyibutsa nomero 3,8, na 31 urabona neza ko icizere bari bagifitiye Imana gusumba ibindi vyose. Hari nâ€™abandi barera amaboko bakigira abanebwe ngo Imana irababona ariko abasogokuru bo bamye bashira imbere ibikorwa raba imyibutsa nomero 2, 34. hari nâ€™iyindi yerekana kwirinda urwanko, ukutihebura, nâ€™ibindi bitari bike.
Reka rero tubasangize iyo twashoboye kwegeranya hanyuma namwe bakunzi bâ€™Ikirundi mudufashe mutwuhirire.
Iyo myibutsa yose dufise usanga ifise ijambo Imana. Ivyo rero cyerekana ikibanza Imana ifise mu mutima wâ€™umurundi. Urabona neza ko Imana ari Rugiravyose koko: Ibikorwa, amatungo, ubuzima, guhanura,nâ€™ibindi.
Twibuke kandi ko Abarundi bahereye kera bemera. Bemera Imana imwe, Nyamwambarizwa hose. Hari abihenda bagira ngo abarundi basenga Kiranga ariko ntivyari vyo. Kiranga yari umuhereji canke umufasha ashikana ibisabisho vyâ€™abarundi ku Mana.
Abarundi baremera kandi ko habaho inyatsi, gurtyo bakemera ko naco gishoboye ari naho tubona hariho ibibi bishika mu buzima bwâ€™umuntu. Ivyo bibi ntibikorwa nâ€™Imana, kuko atakibi kiva ku Mana. Niho baca bemeza ko ikibi, imikoshi, nâ€™ayandi mabi aturuka kuri Rwubarwabigata ariyo Mana mbi; Inyatsi.
Imwe imwe muri iyi myibutsa yasaruwe mugitabu citwa LE DIEU DE NOS PERES, Les sources de la religion traditionnelle du Rwanda et du Burundi, Bernardin MUZUNGU, 1974.

## Amajwi yâ€™ibikoko muÂ Kirundi
**Date:** June 24, 2022 11:16 pm  
**URL:** https://akanyaburunga.wordpress.com/2022/06/24/amajwi-yibikoko-mu-kirundi/

Mu rurimi rwacu, hari amavuga akoreshwa iyo igikoko iki canke kiriya gisohoye ijwi. Ayo rero ntasa kuri kimwe nâ€™ikindi. Mu rurimi rwâ€™Ikirundi, igikoko cose cisangiza irivuga rivuga imvugo yaco. Ngâ€™aya amwe muri yo.
Inka
Duhereye ku nka, igitungwa cubashwe cubashwe cane mu mateka yâ€™igihugu. Amavuga ni: kwaÃ bira, kuboroga, kuroha (igira irwane), kuvumera (iyo irondera inyana yayo ngo iyonse), kwivuga (impfizi), gupfuha.
ak.: Yabigoro iriko irabira, iraboroga, iravumera; nayo Rwamaza iriko irivuga, iravumeza, iraroha.
Imbwa
Ikindi gitungwa cari cari cubashwe mu Burundi. Nayo hakora amavuga: gukuga , kubweja, kugwangwara, kumoka.
ak.: Mugina iriko irakuga, irabweja, iragwangwara, iramoka.
Impene (ihene)
Iki ni ikindi gitungwa cororwa cane. Kwabira, guhebebeza, kuboroga (isuguru iriko ishaka kwimya imvyazi).
Intama
Iyi nayo, co kimwe nâ€™ihene, amavuga ni Kwabira, kuboroga.
Imbeba, inyoni, uduswi
Kujwiragira
Inkoko
Gukokoza, kubika, kwanira (iyo ibangamiwe),guteterera (yimirije guta amagi).
Imbwebwe
Kumoka
Intare
Kuroha
Nkâ€™uko mubibona, hari amajwi avugwa kumwe nko kuboroga mu gihe igikoko kigeramiwe ; kuroha mu gihe kigomba kurwana nâ€™ikindi, kwanira mu gihe bagira bagice izosi. Ayo majwi hari nâ€™ayo bisangiye nâ€™abantu.
Hakaba hari ayandi majwi tutavuze, yadusabikanirize.

## Inyandiko yâ€™Ikirundi: Ibaruwa vs UbutumwaÂ bugufi
**Date:** October 27, 2016 11:47 am  
**URL:** https://akanyaburunga.wordpress.com/2016/10/27/inyandiko-yikirundi-ibaruwa-vs-ubutumwa-bugufi/

Mu bihe vya none, kwandika amabaruwa biriko biraharurukwa. Ikibanza cavyo kiriko gitwarwa nâ€™ubutumwa bugufi haba kuri ngendanwa canke ku ngurukanabumenyi. Nâ€™aho iryo ari iterambere, ntawodeha ko hariho ibitari bike dutakaza kuko tutagikoresha ubwo buryo bwo gutumatumanako na canecane mu nyandiko.
Ishusho: pixabay.com
Aho hambere hahise, ubuhinga bwo gutumatumanako no guhanahana amakuru butaratera imbere, abantu bakoresha amakete ariyo mabaruwa mu kuramutsa abagenzi, incuti canke nyene mu kwitura ibiro bitari bike.
Igihe hakora amabaruwa ntivyari vyoroshe. Ubutumwa bwarateba gushikira uwo bugenewe, canke nyene ntibumushikire canke bugashika bwataye igihe. Abize mu mashure yâ€™uburaro mu bihe biheze, baribuka ko bashobora kurungikirwa ibaruwa rigashika haheze amezi atatu aja ageze gutaha. Atari abayacisha kuri Posita, abandi bayarungikana abantu nabo hari igihe bavyibagira canke bakagira izindi ngorane.
Muri ino minsi, incuti nâ€™abagenzi ntibagikoresha amabaruwa. Aho haziye uduhamagazo na canecane ngendanwa, ubu ukeneye umuntu atamuhamagaye ngo amuvugishe ikibiriraho, amwandikira ubutumwa bugufi. Ubu hoho twateye intambwe nini cane kuko tugeze aho wandikiye umuntu umenya ko ubutumwa bwamushikiriye, yabusomye mbere ariko aranandika ngo agusubize. Â Bica vyumvikana ko amabaruwa atakigira ikibanza.
Akamaro kâ€™amabaruwa
Nâ€™aho yateba, amabaruwa yarafasha mu gutsimbataza ubuhinga bwo kwandika. Turavye ubu ivyandikwa, biramaramaje kuko urabura ururimi birimwo. Birateye isoni kubona. Nkâ€™akarorero, ejo bundi nabonye umuntu yarungitse ikintu ngo:
â€œbit,chr!!!jâ€™wâ€™mpvy shan!gragez wisbrko vreuma.bzbz :)â€
Mbajije ico bisigura ngo ni:
â€œBite ChÃ©rie! Jewe wampevye sha. Gerageza wisubireko vraiement. Bisous! Bisous!â€
Nkâ€™ivyo aho hambere ntivyabaho. Yaba ari uwo mumenyeranye canke uwo mutamenyeranye, uwo usumba canke uwugusumba, wategerezwa kwandika neza ukurikije amategeko yâ€™inyandiko. Ivyo vyarafasha mu guteza imbere ururimi eka mbere no mugukomeza ubushobozi bwo kwandika abantu. Â Abâ€™ubu ntawokwandika umutwe wâ€™amajambo ngo awumare adakoshoje, yaba umugenzi canke imashini canke Kazinduzi.
Ikindi ciza câ€™amabaruwa ni uko wumva neza ijwi ryâ€™uwakwandikiye kuko ivyo bandika vyaba vyitondewe kandi birimwo akanovera, inkumbu nâ€™ikiroroge. Uwandika ibaruwa yaragerageza agashiramwo ivyo vyose biri mu mutima wâ€™iwe, kuburyoÂ bishikiriye uwubisoma wamengo niwe bariko barayaga amaso mu yandi. Ubwo buhinga ntibwari busanzwe kandi burakenye cane mu butumwa bugufi twandikiranira mu bihe vya none.
Ukuntu twandika ubutumwa bugufi biratwengeje cane. Turacagagura, tugasimbagurika mbere nâ€™iciyumviro ntitukimare. Eka uravye, wokwibaza ko atankumbu canke igishika biba birimwo. Icibonekeza ni uko ubu abantu umengo baguma hafi na hafi cane ku buryo inkumbu zica zigabanuka.
Nâ€™aho atawovuga ngo dusubire kwandika amabaruwa, turakwiye kuja turibukiriza.Â Duhiriwe duhishije, amabaruwa aracandikwa ahatari hake. Nâ€™aho bariko barijukira ubuhinga bushasha, abakorera mu biro bitandukanye baracakoresha ubwo buhinga bwâ€™amabaruwa. Nico gituma dukwiye kwiyibutsa ibice bigize amakete mu kirundi kuko icibonekeza ari uko manshi yandikwa mu gifaransa canke mu congereza. Wipfuza kuraba inyubako yâ€™ikete mu kirundi, fyonda ngaha.

## Kumwa ubwanwa iryambere
**Date:** September 5, 2016 2:08 pm  
**URL:** https://akanyaburunga.wordpress.com/2016/09/05/kumwa-ubwanwa-iryambere/

Ubwanwa ni ikimenyetso co gutera intambwe mu buzima bwâ€™umuntu ava mu bwanwa aja mu busore. Iyo umusore ameze ubwanwa, kirazira ko atangura kubumwa adateretse ngo se amurekurire kubumwa iranga umurango izuba ryaka.
Mu buzima bwâ€™abarundi hari ibintu bija biraranga intambwe mu buzima bwâ€™umuntu. Havuye kuvuka, kurongora no kwitaba Imana, hari nâ€™utundi twinshi tuja turaranga urugendo rwâ€™umuntu hano kwâ€™isi. Nâ€™ubu abantu basirimutse, hariho abagira amasabukuru yâ€™amavuko, iminsi mikuru umuntu yaronse urupapuro rwâ€™umutsindo, ukubatizwa, nâ€™ibindi vyinshi. Kera naho, abarundi bakiri abarundi, mu migenzo yâ€™abarundi, hariho ibintu vyinshi vyakorwa. Ico twashimye kubayagira uyu munsi rero ni igikorwa co kumwa ubwanwa bwa mbere.
Ubwanwa, iteka nâ€™ijambo
Umuhungu ameze ubwanwa yaranezerwa cane kandi akabona ko ateye intambwe. Kumera ubwanwa vyerekana gukura, waba washikiriye igihe co gusohoka. Ukitwa serugo, umunega canke umucance. Waba ugiye mu gitigiri câ€™abakuze, mbere waba ugiye mu mugwi wâ€™abatumwajambo. Banakuyeho umwibutsa ngo Â«Â ubwanwa butazi kuvuga bwovuzwa ubuhiriÂ Â»; bisigura ko ubwanwa busanzwe bugaragaza umuntu avuga neza ijambo. Nâ€™aho ubwanwa atariryo jambo, umuntu abufise iyo adashoboye kuvuga ijambo aba asuzuguritse.
Ubwanwa ni ikintu cerekana ko umwana yasoretse. Buri mu bigaragaza ko umuntu avuye mu bwana akaja mu busore. Barayamaze bati ahavuye ubwana hasubira ubwanwa. Ni ikimenyetso câ€™ubugabo. Nâ€™aho hariho abantu batamera ubwanwa nâ€™aho baba bageze, kenshi hapfuma haza buke ariko bukamera.
Ntawumwa ubwanwa atateretse
Aho hambere, ntamusore yubahuka ngo amwe ubwanwa atabirekuriwe nâ€™umuvyeyi. Yakuze, yabona ubwanwa bwagwiriye butakiri impembwe, akitora agasaba se amuvyara atiÂ : Â«Â mpa uruhusha mwe ubwanwa.Â Â» Uwo nawe yaca amutuma kwenga inzoga agatereka bagatumira abantu. Rwaba urubanza nkâ€™izindi senaka agatumira abizigirwa, ababanyi nâ€™abagenzi. Yaraheza akagira umugirwa wo kumumwa ubwanwa bwambere. Kuri uwo munsi nyene yaramuha uruhusha rwo kwama abumwa uko abishatse amajambi akavugwa. Imihezagiro igasekera bamwipfuriza gutera iyindi ntambwe agashinga umuryango. Iyo atagira se yaca abigirirwa na sekuru, se wabo canke uwundi muntu ahumuye mu muryango mu gihe abo bose atawe afise. Ikizira ni uko atawahirahira ngo amwe ubwanwa ubwambere atabumwerewe nâ€™umukurambere.
Insiguro yâ€™uwo mugirwa
Kumwa ubwanwa iryambere ntayindi ntumbero vyari bifise atari ukwereka umusore ko inyundo ikura idasumba iyayujuje. Kumwereka ko abantu baguma bakeneraniye, nâ€™aho akuze ategerezwa kwubaha abamukurira. Abanza gutereka kugire ico kintu gihabwe agaciro kuko iyo ntambwe ari nini cane. Ni naho yahabwa impanuro zâ€™abakuze. Ntikwari ugusesagura, kuko ico gihe baragiha agaciro bidasanzwe.

## Twige ikirundi : IndomeÂ zivuga
**Date:** July 25, 2016 2:54 pm  
**URL:** https://akanyaburunga.wordpress.com/2016/07/25/twige-ikirundi-indome-zivuga/

Mu kirundi turatandukanya indome zigize imvugo hamwe nâ€™inyandiko. Izo nazo hari indome zivuga nâ€™indome zâ€™indagi. Uno munsi twashimye kubashikiriza urutonde rwâ€™indome zivuga.
Indome zivuga ni zitanu (5):
a: Urudome rwa mbere. Mu kuruvuga turasama, imibangabanga igatandukana cane iminwa nayo igasanzarara tugaca dusohora impwemu.
Uturorero: abana, abatwa, amata
i: uru narwo mu kuruvuga turamina iminwa irora mu misaya imibangabanga yegeranye cane. Urashobora no kuruvuga ufatanije amenyo hanyuma ugasohora impwemu.
Uturorero: igiti, imiti, ipikipiki
u: Uru narwo mu kuruvuga dusongora iminwa imibangabanga yegeranye
Uturorero: umuntu, umupfumu, umutwa
o: uru narwo turuvuga dutandukanijeimibangabanga kandi dusongoye iminwa
Uturorero: umutobo, indobo, inkoko
e: Tuyivuga nka i ariko amenyo yâ€™epfo nâ€™aya ruguruÂ  agatandukana bukebuke.
Uturorero: ikete, imeza,
UmvirizaÂ  uko zivurwa ufyonze ngaha hepfo.
Murakoze. Munezerwe no kwiga ururimi rwâ€™ikirundi no kurwigisha.

## Twibukanye Inyandiko yâ€™Ikirundi
**Date:** June 21, 2016 11:36 am  
**URL:** https://akanyaburunga.wordpress.com/2016/06/21/twibukanye-inyandiko-yikirundi/

Nâ€™ubu ntakuruhuka. Dutegerezwa kugumana akarangamutima kâ€™abarundi vyanka bikunda. Umugambi ukurikiyeÂ ; twofata ko ari mushasha, ni ukwibukanya ukuntu ikirundi candikwa. Ubiravye vyibagiwe birenze urugero. Inyandiko nziza isa nâ€™indero nziza. Kandi ururimi rwanditswe ni vyiza kuko ruca rwongereza imyaka yo kubaho.
Ikirundi, co kimwe nâ€™izindi ndimi zose zo kwisi , na canecane izitwa ngo zirakenye zo muri Afirika, kiragoye kwandika. Birababaje kubona umuntu amaramazwa nâ€™uko yanditse nabi ururimi nkâ€™igifaransa canke icongereza (indimi mvamahanga) ariko ikirundi yavykiyemwo acandika nkâ€™ibiyori nâ€™isakamburiraÂ : arucagagura, aruhindagura,â€¦ Wohweje inyandiko iri mu barutse ubu hoho ni akamaramaza.
Vyoba biva kukiÂ ?
Ikirundi candikwa nabi kuko bene kirundi batacitaho. Izindi ndimi nazo usanga hariho za kazinduzi zija ziratwereka uko tuzandika kandi no mu buhinga bwa none barazikoresha cane. Abarundi bati utotsora imfuku yamizayo akatsi, ibindi bihugu vyovyo vyaratahuye ko batagerezwa kwamizako mu gukundisha, mu guteza imbere mbere no kwihabera ururimi rwabo. Uravye nkâ€™icongereza, usanga hariho uburyo bwinshi kandi bworoheje bwo kuciga bitagoranye.
Ikindi naco, ni uko abahinga bacu , abashakashatsi bâ€™abarundi bashira ubuhinga bwabo mu rurimi rwâ€™abanyamahanga. Ivyo bituma umengo ikirundi si ururimi rwâ€™ubushakashatsi, ubuhinga nâ€™ibindi ikomeye. Umengo ni ururimi rwâ€™ibicuba nâ€™amazinaÂ ; kandi rwa kera gusa.
Inguvu rusigaranye
Nâ€™aho ari uko ikirundi kirafise inguvu zitari nke. Amayagwa yarwo araryohera ugutwi bigatanga icizere ko azoguma avurwa mu kirundi. Ikindi naco, hari abantu baguma bitanga. Abo ndabita abarundi bâ€™umutima. Baritangira ururimi mu kurukoresha na ntaryo mu vyo bakora. Abo nabo ni abo badahengeshanya kurukoresha mu biyago, mu mvyino, mu ndirimbo, mu bisabisho, eka nâ€™ahandi. Icongeye ko ni uko hari abantu benshi bamaze gutahura canke bagenda baratahura ko ikirundi gikwiye kugarukirwa.
Umugambi uzomara ikiÂ ?
Kwibukanya inyandiko yâ€™ikirundi bizofasha cane. Bizotuma tubona uko yamajambo twahora duhindagura uko twishakiye tumenya uko yandikwa. Twizeye kandi ko ruzoca rurushirizaho gukoreshwa. Ico twosaba ni uko abahinga boraba ukuntu ururimi rwohinyanyurwaÂ  rukoroshwa. Harakwiye kandi kujaho umugwi ujejwe kugenzura ikoreshwa ryarwo no kuruha agateka. Ikindi gikenewe cane ni uko zina murundi wese yokwitangira ururimi rwiwe ari narwo rutubikiye vyinshi. Akami kâ€™umurundi kari mu kirundi.
Wipfuza gutanga intererano twandikire kuri akanyaburunga@gmail.com

Igikorwa câ€™Umuranzi
Co kimwe no mu myaka ya kera, nâ€™imbere yâ€™umuzo wâ€™uduhamagazo ngendanwa umuranzi yari afise ikibanza kidasanzwe mu guhuza imiryango. Nâ€™uwâ€™ubwoba nta ngorane yagira iyo yaciye ku muranzi.

Bagakora ibishoboka vyose bakamutora atawo mu rupangu wundi abiciye nâ€™ikanda. Nâ€™iyo umukobwa mwamenyanye ntivyoroha ko muhana isango.
None babikora bate?
Adolf, ni umugabo wâ€™imyaka 35 yavukiye kandi akurira mu gisagara ca Bujumbura. Ku vyerekeye ugukundana kwiwe ( copinage) biratwengeje cane nkâ€™uko avyivugira.Â  â€œ Natanguye kuresha mfise imyaka mike cane. Nari aga smart boy.Â  Umukobwa twavugana rimwe nagenda yanyemeye.
