## #Menya akahise kawe: Bihome umutabazi wâ€™umwami MweziÂ Gisabo
**Date:** May 25, 2018 6:00 pm  
**URL:** https://akanyaburunga.wordpress.com/2018/05/25/menya-akahise-kawe-bihome-umutabazi-wumwami-mwezi-gisabo-2/

Kumenya akahise neza bifasha gutegura akazoza keza. Muri buno butohozi bwa mbere, twipfuje kubayagira ku muntu ahambaye cane mu Burundi. Umuntu yiguze igihugu izuba riva, yagwaniye agateka kâ€™igihugu ciwe, atuma Uburundi bwubahwa mbere bugumana iteka.Â  Uwo muntu ni umutabazi Bihome.
Izina rya Bihome ritangura kuvugwa inyuma yâ€™umuzo wâ€™abazungu, mu ntango yâ€™ikinjana ca mirongo ibiri. Ubuzima bwiwe bwâ€™imbere yâ€™aho ntaco babuvugako. Icibonekeza gusa ni uko yari umwishikira i bwami. Â Ishusho yonyene abonekako (nkâ€™uko babivuga) iravyerekana. Aboneka yicaye i buryo bwa Mwezi Gisabo, Â inyuma yâ€™abazungu babiri bâ€™ivyanwa birebire bacagatiye umwami Mwezi. Aho hantu aboneka neza ko atariko arya ifyeri ryo gufotorwa, ahubwo yasa nâ€™uwucunze ngo ivyo bishema ntibihinduke umwami. Ivyo birerekana ko ikibanza Bihome yari afise i bwami kitari gisanzwe.
Iyo foto yafashwe nâ€™abasesankomoko, mu gifaransa â€œantropologuesâ€, baturuka mu gihugu câ€™ubudagi, igihe bariko bariga uko abarundi babayeho. Tubibutse ko abakoloni, imbere yo gutangura gucura bufuni na buhoro igihugu ico arico cose, babanza kurungika abasesamiryango babo bakaciga bacegereye. Bamaze kumenya uko abantu baho babayeho, baca bazana abigisha ijambo ryâ€™Imana. Abo rero baza babashishitira bakabakwegakwega babaryosharyosha kugire bashobore kubashira ku murongo wabo. Barababwira ngo bahebe imigenzo yabo yo gusenga no kwemera Imana babahenda ngo ijana mu muriro. Bamaze kubigarurira, haza ingabo, zizananye nâ€™abaje gushinga intwaro. Â No mu Burundi vyagenze uko.
Ubutwari bwa Bihome bwagaragaye muri ico kiringo ca gatatu câ€™ukwinjiranwa. Igihe abadagi bariko bararwana nâ€™ingabo zâ€™umwami zikoresha umuheto nabo bakoresha ibikoho bikomakomeye, vyaraboneka ko umwami ageramiwe. Kubera ubukomezi bwâ€™ abadasigana, ingabo zâ€™umwami, abadagi babaye nkâ€™abariye amavubi. Baje ata kindi bagamije atari kugandagura umwami. Bari bamaze kubura benshi babo, mu ndwano hagati na bo nâ€™ingabo zâ€™umwami. Ko bari babonye bashitse ku kirimba câ€™umwami wâ€™Uburundi, bagire babukore mu jisho. Abanyamabanga barakoranye, umwami Mwezi Gisabo aranyegera. Abadagi baramuhize hasi hejuru ariko ntibamwuva ishwashwa.
Niko guca baja barabaririkiza, mu mihana uwoba azi irengero ryiwe. Bahavuye baronka ibimenabanga bivuga ko umwami amaze iminsi kwa Bihome. Baca bajayo, urugo bararukikuza. Umwami yabona ko ubwiwe buheze. Ariko Bihome igihe ciwe co gutabara igihugu cari kigeze. Yafashe impuzu zâ€™umwami Mwezi, arazambara, aca arasohoka asoboka nkâ€™uwutorotse. Aho yagomba abamubona bibaze ko ari umwami Mwezi ariko agerageza kuyanyaga.Â  Bamwe bari bakikuje urugo rwiwe ntibatevye kumuja mu nyuma ngo bahekure Uburundi.
Abasirikare bâ€™abadagi barongowe na Bwana Birenge, ni bo bakurikiye Bihome gushika bamugandaguye nâ€™amasase menshi cane ku mutumba Nkomwe muri Komine Kiganda. Abadagi bose bari mu Burundi bariruhukije bazi ko bagaritse Umwami. Bandikira umwami Keizer bamubwira bati: Umwami wâ€™uburundi twamugaritse, ubu igihugu cose tugifise mu ntoke.
Abadagi aho bumviye ko ingoma yagumye ivumera, bakamenya ko bishe Bihome atari Mwezi Gisabo, bariyanse. Â Baremeye umwami aguma aganje ariko bakoresha igikenye, nkâ€™uko tuzobibashikirako mu kiganiro cacu câ€™ubutaha, baramunyaga.
Kugira ube kirumara mu gihugu ntibisaba ngo ube uri iki canke kiriya. Bihome ntiyari mu ngabo zâ€™umwami canke ngo abe no mu nda yâ€™ingoma. Ariko, mu mwanya muto cane yarakoze birashimwa. Kugeza ubu igihugu kiracitwa Uburundi kandi abadagi bashaka bacigarurire.
Ivyo Bihome yakoze ntivyari vyoroshe. Ariko aho hagoye nyene, ni ho yaciye gushika ageze kukitamuryohera ariko kizoryohera abarundi imyaka nâ€™imyaka.
Umwami yahavuye yerekana ko ivyo uwo yakoze ataho bigegwa, mu kumushira ku rutonde rwâ€™abatabazi. Ikibanza kitari bwigere kijamwo umuntu atari mu nda yâ€™ingoma. Yaratahuye ko Bihome atiguze Mwezi Gisabo, nyabuna yiguze igihugu. Umuryango wiwe yarawuninahaje, awugabira ryaka nkâ€™uko yabigirira abandi. Ingabire yatanze ni zo zahavuye zivamwo ingoma Murimirwa na Ruciteme, ingoma nâ€™ubu zikiri mu kigabiro co mu Gishora.
Bihome yavukiye ku mutumba Kanegwa I Kiganda, umutumba wahoze witwa Buturirwa. Yavutse mu muryango wâ€™abajiji umwe mu miryango yâ€™abahutu bâ€™abanyamabanga i bwami.

Izina â€œBareraâ€ rirakunda gokoreshwa mu kirundi ryongewe ku yandi majambo rikaba iryungikane. Ivyo bituma umuntu yibaza vyinshi kuri iryo zina nâ€™ayo majambo arikomokako. Akibaza nimba Barera yari umuntu, nâ€™ivyamuranze bigatuma avugwa nkâ€™uko.
Ishusho: Youtube
Izina Barera abaroranya imvugo na kahise bohava barishira ku ntwaro ya gikoroni aho abazungu baza gucura bufuni na buhoro Afirika yari yiganziwe nâ€™ubwami butandukanye nâ€™ingoma yâ€™Uburundi irimwo. Aho boba bafatiye ku mvugo yâ€™iryo zina yegeranye na ca gisagara câ€™Ubudagi caberamwo inama yâ€™amagaburabutaka yo 1885. Ico gisagara citwa Berile; umuntu yokwibaza ko arico nkomoko yâ€™irya jambo Barera na canecane ko ariho havuye akabi kose karuhije basogokuru. Canakwira nâ€™abadagi nibo baciye biyizira gucunaguza abarundi; kandi kanatsinda nâ€™iryo zina Barera rikunze kwungikanywa nâ€™amabi gusa.
Ihibambewe, mu matohoza twagize twasanze Barera yari umuntu kandi ataho ahuriye nâ€™ubukoroni kuko yari umurundi. Abatohozi bâ€™imico nâ€™imigenzo na Kahise twabajije batubwiye ko Barera yari umuntu atonye cane I bwami.
Ingoma yâ€™umukazo udasanzwe
Ngo hari ku ngoma yâ€™umwami Mwambutsa III Mbonuburundi batazira Nyamubi (1732-1740). Iryo zina ryâ€™iritazirano yarihawe kubera ukuntu yagisibije mu co yaramutswa. Yarangaje abantu, abandi arabanyaga eka mbere nâ€™abaganwa aragarika.Â  Abakera baremeza ko ingoma yiwe yararemereye abarundi bidasanzwe.
Turamaze kwumva ko Abambutsa bari bamenyereye kutiha ubuki nkâ€™abandi bami, nkâ€™abatare nâ€™abezi hamwe nâ€™abataga.Â  Abambutsa bose bahereza kwambuka bakaja gusazira kure yâ€™ubwami. Mwambutsa Nyamubi rero yipfuje kudeha iryo ragi agomba gusaza aganza mu Burundi kandi atihaye ubuki. Ivyo ntivyanezera abarundi kuko babona ariko ararenga indahiro. Abahanuzi baramuhanura akica amatwi.

## Yaga akaranga: KwÃ®menjura
**Date:** February 16, 2017 10:55 am  
**URL:** https://akanyaburunga.wordpress.com/2017/02/16/yaga-akaranga-kwimenjura/

Gukora ikosa mu kibano ni ibara. Birahanwa cane nâ€™amateka yâ€™abarundi. Iyo umuntu yakoze ikosa, bavuga ko yamenje. Uwo vyashikiye, abarundi ntibaca bamuta. Baramuha umwanya wo kwirimbura mbere akanafata ingingo yo kwisubiza mu bantu ku bushake bwiwe. Ivyo nivyo bita kwimenjura. SomaÂ  mwumve ukwo vyagenda nâ€™akamaro kavyo.
Ishusho: Ubushinguro bwa Youtube
Mu kibano, ibintu ntivyama vyera ngo de! Karacamwo ugasanga bararabanye ribi, bakavugana nabi eka mbere bakana gwana. Na none barayamaze ngo â€œntazibana zidakubitana amahembe.â€ Ibituma zikubitana amahembe navyo ntawobidondagura ngo abimare. Vyinshi bikunze kubaho ni amatati aya canke ariya, uguhemuka canke nyene akisandagazo.
Igihe cose bibaye haba hariho umuntu umwe ari mu kuri nâ€™uwurenganywa; inkwezi yâ€™amarere nâ€™uwabikwegewemwo.Â  Abo nibo bikenewe ko basubizwa hamwe bagasubira kwumvikana babona kumwe ibintu. Iyo bidashobotse, ibintu biguma vyunyuka, hakavukiramwo ingorane nyinshi.
Amakosa arasumbana. Hari iryo umuntu akora bikaboneka ko risanzwe mbere iryo ntirigora kuzimangana. Ayo ni nko guhonyora ku muntu utamubonye, kuvuga nabi izina ryiwe, nâ€™ibindi. Hari nâ€™ayandi akomeye cane. Nko kwica umuntu, gutukana vyenyuje, kwiba, kurementaniriza umuntu, nâ€™ibindi vyinshi. Ayo nayo aragorana kukosora.
Amakosa amwe amwe, bivanye nâ€™uko akorwa kenshi kandi ashikira benshi, abarundi bahitamwo kuyababarira bitagoranye nâ€™aho yoba akomeye. Aho ni nko kwoneshereza umubanyi. Kubera bose bishika kuko batunze inka, barumva ko hamwe bagiye bararihisha bosanga bagumye mwâ€™ihorihori.
Mu bisanzwe, ikosa ryose rikosorwa nâ€™indishi yâ€™akababaro. Ariko inzira nziza yo gusubiza hamwe abatase, ni uko umwe muri bo yemera ko yakoze ikosa mbere akanabisabira imbabazi. Iyo atari ikosa rihambaye cane, gusaba ikigongwe bivuye ku mutima vyâ€™ukuri birakwiye. Ariko igihe naho ikosa rigoye kubabarira, indishi yâ€™akababaro ntikwiye. Hari ikindi uwagiriwe nâ€™ikosa yasabwa.
Ikibanza câ€™abashingantahe
Abashingantahe nibo bamye, kuva kera, bafasha abantu kwumva ko naka ariwe yatiriganye kwâ€™ibanga canke ari naka wundi. Igihe cose habaye amatati, turamenyereye twumva ngo baca baja mu bagabo. Ivyo busigura ko baca bahamagara intahe igasasa ikumviriza abantu mbere ikagenda ibonye aho ukuri kuri. Uwagiriwe nâ€™ikosa agatanga agatutu akongera agahanurwa, barayamaze ngo intahe ntihana irunga.
Hari amakosa batapfa kurekerana ukwo. Iyo babona ari irikomeye, barasaba uwarikoze kwimenjura. Kwari ugutereka ukagira umunsi mukuru wo kwisubiza mu bantu.
Ukwimenjura uko vyangenda
Uwimenje yaramara iminsi yaraciwe mu bantu. Bavuga ko bamuciriye umukenke. Ntiyasangira inzoga nâ€™abandi, kandi iyo asomyeko ntawayisubira, nâ€™aho yaba ari umwana muto. Iyo agiye mu rubanza rwâ€™umubanyi, ntibamwima ariko yanywera ukwâ€™iwe ahinyegeje. Bamuha mu rwato rwâ€™iwe gusa iyasigara bakayibogora. Ntawayisubizamwo umukenke. Urwato narwo baca barubika bakazorwoza cane. Birumvikana neza ko yaba amerewe nabi mu kibano.
Yarushe, yarasaba abashingantahe bakamuha umunsi mwiza wo kwimenjura. Uwo munsi yarenga intango, agatereka, ukaba umunsi mukuru. Umunsi wo gusubira mu bantu. Haraza umushingantahe mukuru ku mutumba amajambo akavugwa hanyuma bakamusubiza mu bantu ku mugaragaro. Kera uko vyakorwa, bavuga ko bamutota imiti yo kumurtyorora ariko uko iminsi yagiye irahera, bagye barakoresha amajambo canecane. Yaraheza agasubira akaba umuntu mu bandi, akagendana nâ€™abandi, bagatizanya ivyo batizanya, ubuzima bugasubira. Nâ€™abantu barahanahana bakavuga ko kanaka yimenjuye bagaheza bagasubira bakamwiyumvamwo.
Inyuma yâ€™inzoga, amajambo nâ€™ibindi bikorwa umunsi wo kwimenjura, hari ikindi gihambaye bifasha. Kwimenjura ni ubwambere na mbere vyerekana ko umuntu yemeye ikosa kandi afashe ingingo yo kuriheba. Ikindi ni uko umuntu yumva ko ivyaheze biheze atanguye ubundi buzima. Uwo munsi utuma umuntu asubira kunagura urukundo nâ€™umubano umuhuje nâ€™abo babana. Ikindi congeyeko, ni uko kwimenjura bituma abantu batinya amakosa bigatuma ubuzima bugenda neza mu kibano.

## BurundiÂ : umunyu wa kera nâ€™ukuntuÂ wahingurwa
**Date:** June 10, 2025 2:06 pm  
**URL:** https://akanyaburunga.wordpress.com/2025/06/10/burundi-umunyu-wa-kera-nukuntu-wahingurwa/

Uwu munyu dufungura uno musi ntiwamyeho mu Burundi. Hari nyabuna uwundi witwa umugonzo canke umushanga. Uwo munyu hari benshi batazi uko wahingurwa, ndetse batanazi nâ€™uko wabaho. Tugira tubibagire ku muriri twifashishije ivyo twasigiwe nâ€™umwanditsi Vekemans, ari we yatubereye isÃ´ko mu gitabu ciwe Â«Â Burundi Traditionnel, aperÃ§u sur les relations familialesÂ Â». Naho nawe nyene atavuze vyinshi, ivyo yavuze biratwungurura amaso tukabona uburyo nâ€™ubuhinga bwa sogokuru.
Mark Kurlansky mu gitabu ciwe yanditse citwa â€œSalt: A World Historyâ€ yerekana ukuntu umunyu usigura ibintu bitandukanye mu mico itandukanye: rimwe na rimwe ukaba ikimenyetso câ€™ubutore, ubwitonzi canke ubutunzi. Isinzi ryâ€™abantu ba kera bawufata nkâ€™igitangaza, aho mu mico myinshi gusangira umunyu vyari ikimenyetso câ€™ubucuti nâ€™ugushikirana.
Mu Burundi, nimbaÂ  hari ikirungo cariÂ  kigoye ironka, harimwo nâ€™umunyu. Birerekana ko wari ikintu câ€™agaciro cane, gushika nâ€™aho abakoroni hamwe nâ€™abamisiyonari bawukoresha nkâ€™igikoresho co guhendesha abanyagihugu, kugira babemerere kuba mu Burundi no gushikira inyungu zabo. Umupatiri Vekemans yanditse ko uwu munyu dusanzwe turya uno musi utariho. Kenshi bawuronka bavuye kurobera i Uvinza.
Mu Burundi bwo hambere wavahe ? Wahingurwa gute?
Umunyu aho hambere wari nkâ€™ umuzi wâ€™ibuye. Abarundi bakera bahingura umunyu uzwi kwâ€™izina ryâ€™ â€œumushangaâ€. Mu kuwuhingura, barafata ubwatsi burandarandaÂ  mu mazi buzwi nkâ€™ â€œumuragoâ€ canke â€œumugonzoâ€,Â  bakabuturira maze umunyota watwo bakawushira mu mazi, hanyuma amaziÂ  akamiminwa akavangurwa na wa munyota ugakoreshwa mu kurunga ibifungurwa.
Hari nâ€™ubundi bwatsi buzwi nkâ€™ â€œumukangagaâ€(carex mu gifaransa), nâ€™ubwo barabwanikiraÂ  indwi yose canke irenga, hanyuma bakabucucagira amazi, bagaca babukanyura kugira havamwo amazi asosa bayakoresha mu mfungurwa. Hari nâ€™ubundi buryo bahinguramwo umukangaga.Â  Barawumisha imisi igera kuri cumi nâ€™itanu, bakawuturira hanyuma umunyota uvuyemwo usosagirika ukaba ari wo barungisha infungurwa.

Benshi babwiketse baca biruka kwinyegeza. Â Mu kubimenyesha, bavuza ingoma bahererekanya kugeza igihugu cose cinyegeje.

## #Inkingi zâ€™akaranga: Ntiharirizwa Innocent, ruremeshangabo mu mugwi ndangakaranga â€œAmagabaâ€
**Date:** October 3, 2018 5:50 pm

Afise ijwi ridasanzwe. Ahibongoje abantu bata amacumu. Iyo ari mu giteramo ntawutaha kitarangiye kuko atosiga iyo ntarambira yandamye kunezereza abatumire. Ntiharirizwa I.

Kuva akiri muto nâ€™igihe cose yariko avuza ingoma, na canecane aho atanguriye ibanga ryâ€™ukuvyina yagumye yiga nâ€™ibindi bicurarangisho vyâ€™ikirundi. Yize umuduri, ikembe, nâ€™ibindi. Abo bose aguma abashimira cane kuko bamufashije bidasanzwe.
Ishingwa ryâ€™umugwi amagaba
Ari kumwe nâ€™abandi bagenzi (imisore nâ€™inkumi) bakunda akaranga, bagiye inama yo gushinga umugwi ndangakaranga ufise intumbero tubona uno munsi ku mbuga koraniro nâ€™imboneshakure. Bipfuza gushinga ishirahamwe rimwe ryâ€™akarorero mu Burundi, muri Afurika eka mbere no mu makungu. Niko gushinga umugwi ubahuza bose mu ngabire zose bafise: amajwi atosoye, ubuhinga bwo kuvuza ivyuma, nâ€™ibindi. Batanguye ibikorwa igenekerezo rya 5 Rusama 2014. Mu minsi ya mbere vyaragoranye kubera ibihe igihugu carimwo ariko kuva 2016 nkâ€™uko Stephanie Soleansky yahora aserukira ikigo ndangamico câ€™abafaransa avyemeza, uwo mugwi ntiwasivye kwerekana ibitangaza mu kuzana dushasha mu karanga nâ€™umudiho wâ€™ikirundi.
Bariyumviriye izina bita uwo mugwi baca bahuriza kwâ€™izina â€œAmagÇbaâ€. Izina rikomoka kwâ€™igÇba, icumu baha samuragwa, ari naryo ryamye riranga abashingantahe. Ni rirya cumu riherekeza abatimbo canke rikabaja imbere. Kubwâ€™abo banyakaranga, igaba ni ikimenyetso cereka â€œubutore nâ€™ubutwariâ€. Kubera bari benshi baciye bitwa AmagÇba.

Abamuzi bemeza ko ari umukozi adasanzwe kandi ataruha. Ubutwari bwâ€™iwe nâ€™ubushobozi buguma bugaragara mu bikorwa vyâ€™umugwi Amagaba, no mu giteramo â€œUmukozoâ€ ( Câ€™incuro ya mbere) yarerekanye ubuhinga budasanzwe aho yabonetse atamba ingoma, intore, avyina ,â€¦
Uruvyino Amagaba rwanitswe na Ntiharirizwa Innocent
Ngo ntibimugora kwiyumvira uruvyino. Bimuzamwo aho aba ari hose: mu muduga, mu nzira, aruhutse, eka umwanya wose. Atari abarundi bo nyene bahaye agaciro akaranga kabo, ntabandi bazobikora. Abategura amasabukuru bogerageza bagashiramwo imico yâ€™iwacu. Ngo amaradiyo nâ€™ibimenyeshamakuru navyo vyogerageza bigaha ikibanza kinini akaranga kâ€™iwacu no kugahayagiza. Nayo Reta, ngo yogerageza igafasha biboneka abariko barateza imbere akaranga.

## Umukozo 2018: igiteramo câ€™akanovera kadasanzwe câ€™umugwi ndangakarangaÂ â€œAmagabaâ€
**Date:** June 12, 2018 11:05 am  
**URL:** https://akanyaburunga.wordpress.com/2018/06/12/umukozo-2018-igiteramo-cakanovera-kadasanzwe-cumugwi-ndangakaranga-amagaba/

Kwâ€™igenekerezo rya 8 Ruheshi 2018, abanyakaranga bâ€™umugwi ndangakaranga Amagaba barerekanye igiteramo kidasanzwe bise â€œUmukozoâ€. Mu buhinga budasanzwe, bahuje umurisho nâ€™intambo yâ€™intore, ikintu kitari bwa boneke mu Burundi. Abatari bahari, barahomvye. Ariko muri make ni bumve uko vyari bimeze aho mu kigo ndangakaranga câ€™ubufaransa mu Burundi kuri uwo mugoroba.
Ishusho: Amagaba
Buragorovye. Mu nyubakwa zâ€™ikigo ndangakaranga câ€™ubufaransa, abantu barakinje. Barakeye mu maso kandi urabona ko biteze ikintu kibanezereye. Bamwe baricaye abandi barahagaze. Hari nâ€™abaja baragendagenda. Inzu yâ€™ibiteramo yari yugaye. Ariko ku mwanya ku mwanya wumva ivyuma bivuga nâ€™amajwi yâ€™abantu. Ahari ivyapa bimenyesha intone zâ€™ibiteguwe muri ico kigo, abantu baguma baza bitegereza. Muri ivyo vyapa, harimwo ikimenyesha igiteramo Umukozo (I) câ€™umugwi ndangakaranga â€œAmagabaâ€. Ico nico baguma baraba badashigwa. Barasoma, bagaca basubira bagatembera bukebuke bataja kure yâ€™umuryango.
Igiteramo câ€™agakura
Igihe kigeze, nkâ€™uko bahora babikora, ikengeri iravuga. Bugurura imiryango abantu baca barundana ku muryango binjira kugira ntibabure ibibanza. Huzuye, bugaye imiryango igiteramo kiratangura. Hatanguye umurisho. Ingoma zirimirikanya zirakubita ikiniro riruzura. Mu nyuma haje intore zinyiririka mu murisho wâ€™ingoma baratamba abari aho baratamarirwa.
Hakurikiye intambo zâ€™abana bâ€™abigeme bâ€™imiyabaga. Abo nabo baratangaje benshi. Barivunagura ukamengo ntibagiramwo igufa na rimwe. Imiyabaga isa neza ireha nkâ€™uko yoba yaciwe ku giti kimwe. Vyari bibereye ijisho. Vyaraboneka ko bakoze bidasanzwe. Umwanya wose, urwungikane rwâ€™ibicurarangisho vyâ€™ikirundi nirwo rwaguma rwumvikana intambo imwe igahera iyindi ikaza, abakobwa bahava hagaruka abahungu.
Nâ€™igihe atawaba ariko aratamba, amajwi arongorotse yâ€™abavyinyi bâ€™umugwi Amagaba, ahujwe mu buhinga budasanzwe nâ€™ibicurarangisho kirundi vyari bibereye ijisho nâ€™ugutwi. Abantu bose bari bahari ntibahengeshanya gukoma amashi bakenguruka ivyiza bariko barabona imbere yabo, bashimira abo bantu bariko badufasha kwibuka akarangamutima kamye karanga zina murundi. Imyironge, umurya wâ€™inanga, indonongo, ikembe, umuduri, ntiwari kwumviriza.
Nkâ€™uko babisiguye, â€œUmukozoâ€ ni ihuriro ryâ€™intambo nâ€™imidiho Kirundi myinshi bahurije mu giteramo kimwe kurya kwâ€™ubugari nâ€™inkozo zabwo bigaca biryoha. Kukaba nkako baratembereje abari aho mu ntara zose zâ€™igihugu nâ€™imidiho itandukanye ihabarizwa.
Akaryo ko gushimira intwari
Igiteramo umukozo catumye haboneka akaryo ko gushimira abantu bose bafashije umugwi Amagaba gushika aho ushitse uno munsi. Babanje gusaba agacerere bibuka umuhisi yahora muri uwo mugwi yitavye Imana, bamusabira ku mana ngo imugumize i buryo bwayo. Mu nyuma baciye batangura gushimira abantu bose bafashije kwigisha ibicurarangisho vyâ€™ikirundi amagaba yose yari aho abakuza ubwatsi.
Icari kiryoshe ni uko hari abarundi batari bake abato nâ€™abakuze, ndetse nâ€™abanyamahanga kandi bose baryohewe cane. Ikibabaje gusa ni uko uravye abanyakaranga bari muri kino gihugu canke abandi banyatugenegene batari benshi nkâ€™uko umuntu yari avyiteze. Bikaboneka ko ico gushigikirana mu banyatugenegene kitarakomera cane. Impinga iracari ndende ariko abari bahari baratuma umuntu yokwizera ko bizoteba bikagenda neza. Abarundi bagashigikira akaranga atawusigaye inyuma nabo abagwanirakaranga bagasenyera ku mugozi umwe.
Igiteramo carangiye mu kanyamuneza ntangere, abantu badashaka ko gihera. Baciye batanga isango mu mwaka uza wa 2019 aho igiteramo â€œUmukozo IIâ€ kizosubira kikaba muri ico kibanza nyene nâ€™uburyohe ntangere. Abantu bumva ari kera, baguma basaba ko bobasubiriramwo ico nyene bakoze.

Izo ndirimbo uko zirutana mu myaka, niko vyumvikanye ko zisumbanya akanovera. Uko imyaka yagiye ikura, niko akanovera kagiye karagabanuka. Ururirimbo rwo mu 2017 nta butumwa na bumwe bwumvikanyemwo, ku bari ngaho. Â Nâ€™ikirundi cavugwamwo nticari gikwiye. â€œCari giteye amazi!â€, nkâ€™uko umwe yabivuze yitwengera. Urwo mu 1990 rwari rurimwo ubutumwa bwumvikana kandi rukozwe ku ngereranyo nâ€™impinyanyuro nyinshi, akaba ari nayo nzira yo kwerekana ubwiza bwâ€™ururimi rwâ€™ikirundi.
Agashavu bamwe bamwe bari bafise ni ukuntu amaradiyo yubahuka akavuza indirimbo zitagira akanovera nkâ€™urwo rwo mu 2017. Ariko iyo nkazabiyago yarabishuye kuko bose batahuye ko amaradiyo avuza ivyo aronse. Hamwe abarundi twisubiyeko tugakora amayagwa yâ€™akanovera, ntakibuza ko amaradiyo aca avuza ivyâ€™akanovera.
Twasezeranye ku mwimenyerezo wo kwandika inkuru ngufi mu Kirundi, nâ€™akakino umunota wâ€™ikirundi, aho umwe wese yahabwa umunota umwe avuga ikirundi kitavanze.
Ni aho ku ndwi iza!

## â€œAri hehe? â€œJean PierreÂ Ngendanzi
**Date:** December 9, 2016 1:29 pm  
**URL:** https://akanyaburunga.wordpress.com/2016/12/09/ari-hehe-jean-pierre-ngendanzi/

Ntawutavyibuka. Umuririmvyi Jean Pierre Ngendanzi yaratumaze irungu kandi nâ€™ubu akiriko. Aka karirimbo karyohera ugutwi kakanyura umutima kandi kigisha, katuvunira urugohe. Insiguro yako yoba ari iyihe?
Umuntu avugwa muri aka karirimbo ni â€œumukobwaâ€. Ijambo rifise insiguro nyinshi bivanye nâ€™aho rikoreshejwe. Rishobora gusigura umuntu wâ€™igitsinagore afise imyaka mike, umwana wa naka (umukobwa wiwe) canke nyene umukunzi. Ni iyo nsiguro yanyuma uwo muririmvyi yavuzemwo uwo muntu.
Umuririmvyi atuyagira inkuru yâ€™umukobwa bahora bakundana ariko abonye uwâ€™amahera menshi aca aramuheba. Ajana nâ€™uwo wâ€™amahera, amaherezo aca aba mabi cane: uwo mushasha yaramutaye amusigarana imvuka. Birumvikana ko yamusigaranye amarira kuko yahakwa gutabwa mu gisumanyenzi canke agacibwa. Ntawuyobewe ukuntu abarundi batahura gutwara ishushu.
Ururirimbo ruratwigisha cane ko mu buzima atawoja arakurikira amaronko. Rutwigisha kandi ko umukene ataba akenye umutima, kuko imyaka yose bari bamaranye nâ€™uwo muririmvyi batari bwagwe mwâ€™isanganya ribatandukanya. Bisigura ko umuririmvyi wewe yari afise umutima azi kugera akageranuza.
Ugurura mwiyumviririze ururirimbo mukurikirane nâ€™amajambo arugize!

## Imvyino, Indirimbo :Â Itandukaniro
**Date:** April 8, 2016 5:15 pm  
**URL:** https://akanyaburunga.wordpress.com/2016/04/08/imvyino-indirimbo-itandukaniro/

AmajamboÂ : imvyino (mu rudende Â«Â uruvyinoÂ Â») na indirimbo (mu rudende Â«Â ururirimboÂ Â») arakunda kwitiranywa iyo abantu bariko barayakoresha mu buzima bwa minsi yose. Kenshi urasanga biva ku mvo nyinshi harimwo ibikoresho vyâ€™umuziki (haba guhinyanyura canke gushira ahabona imvyino canke indirimbo) bisigaye bikoreshwa vyatumye imvyino nâ€™indirimbo birushirizaho gushusha. Ariko, bisanzwe bitandukanye kandi nâ€™ubu hariho ibimenyetso vyinshi bitandukanya imvyino nâ€™indirimbo.
Ishusho:Akanyaburunga
Mu Burundi hoba hatanguye imvyino. Ariko haraja haricangamwo nâ€™indirimbo ariko ku rugero rutari runini cane. Ivyo bibonekera mu mvyino za kera twumvana abasogokuru na ba nyogokuru. Uravye i mbere yâ€™umuzo wâ€™abazungu, usanga akajwi gahibongoje kose kajana ku mvyino gusumba ku ndirimbo. Aha bigaragazwa nâ€™uko nâ€™igitabu cegeranya izo mvyino bise agahogo kâ€™abarundi ciganziye imvyino.
Igihe haje abazungu, ubuhinga bwaciye butera i mbere. Ihinduka riraba, abantu batangura kuja mu masengero aho guhayagiza Imana haba mu misa, ibihimbazo eka mbere no ku minsi mikuru yose wasanga imvyino ziriko ziratanga ikibanza ku ndirimbo. Mu masengero menshi, ibikoresho biboneka kuri gusa. Nkâ€™ibitari, inanga, mbere nâ€™ibindi bicurarangisho, ababikeneye babironka kuri gusa. Ivyo nivyo bituma indirimbo zifata ikibanza kinini gusumba imvyino, na cane cane ko ziba zihinyanyuye ku buhinga buhanitse.
Ikimenyesha ko igikorwa cahinyanyuwe ari uruvyino canke ari ururirimbo ni iki?
Ururirimbo umuntu arumenyera kwipanga nâ€™ihuzwa ryâ€™amajwi: irya mbere, irya kabiri, irya gatatu, niâ€™irya kane. Irya mbere nâ€™irya gatatu avugirwa hejuru cane, irya kane nâ€™irya kabiri nayo akavugirwa hasi. Uyateranije, usanga havuka urusobekerane rwâ€™amajwi aryohera ugutwi ugasanga wohora urumviriza. Uru ririmbo kandi urumenyeshwa nâ€™uko ibitero nâ€™ivyitabirizo biba bigenda kumwe (rimwe na rimwe).
Uruvyino narwo turumenyeshwa nâ€™ibice bibiri vyama biruranga: igitero nâ€™icitabirizo. Kenshi, ivyitabirizo birashobora kuba ari bibiri: icitabirizo rusangi, nâ€™icitabirizo kâ€™inkorahato. Ikindi kirutandukanya nâ€™indirimbo ni uko uruvyino ruvurwa mwâ€™ijwi rimwe kandi rihibongojwe. Kera uruvyino rwerekanwa nâ€™uko bakoresha amashi mu gucuraranga. Amashi aragumya neza nkâ€™ibindi bicurarangisho. Afasha cane cane kutanga umudiho wâ€™uruvyino canke ururirimbo.
Uturorero twerekana itandukaniro ryâ€™uruvyino nâ€™ururirimbo

## Intambo zâ€™ikirundi: igisuru
**Date:** March 25, 2016 12:49 am  
**URL:** https://akanyaburunga.wordpress.com/2016/03/25/intambo-zikirundi-igisuru/

Muri wa mugambi wâ€™akanyaburunga wo kubamenyesha vyinshi ku karanga kâ€™uburundi, nâ€™ubu nyene twashimye kubayagira ku ntambo. Uno munsi dushimye kubayagira ku ntambo yitwa â€œIgisuruâ€. Igisuru gitambwa heheÂ ? cashitse mu burundi ryariÂ ? Gitambwa na bandeÂ ? Mbega intambo yâ€™igisuru isigura ikiÂ ? Yoba yaratambwa i bwamiÂ ? Ivyo ni ibibazo tuja kurabira hamwe muri iki kiyago.
Ni intambo itambwa nâ€™igitsina gabo, kuva ku bahungu batoya gushika ku bisumbuye mugabo bakibasha. Yatambwa mu ntara kama yâ€™ubweru na kumoso ahari intara za Cankuzo, Ruyigi na Rutana. Benshi bavuga ko yoba yaje ituruka mu bihugu vya tanzaniya mu ntara ya Buha. Hari nâ€™abavuga ko yoba yatambwa nâ€™abatwa.
Abayitamba bakoresha umubiri wose na cane cane amafyinga. Iyo abagabo batamba igisuru abagore nabo baba bariko batamba umutsibo. Umudiho wayo urihuta cane nkâ€™uwâ€™ihuruma nâ€™umuyebeÂ . Bayitamba basimbagurika, amaboko bayapfunyapfunya intoke zishamaje neza kurya kwâ€™inyamaswa igomba ifate ikintu. Hari nâ€™igihe baja barasa nâ€™abaterera inyuma yabo utuntu kurya kwâ€™abarimyi bariko barakangaza baterera urwiri inyuma.
Ni intambo igaragaza umunezero abantu baba bafise. Yashobora kugaragaza umunezero wâ€™uwibarutse, umwimbu, inka yavyaye iriza, canke ku zindi manza zose zitunganywa mu miryango. Intambo yâ€™igisuru yakunda gutambwa kenshi ku mpeshi, mukaba muzi ko impeshi abantu baba bimbuye ubwishaza, ingano nâ€™ibiharage. Baba bariko barigina umwimbu. Yaratambwa mbere no ku mutasuro. Muca mwumva ko ari intambo yâ€™umunezero.
Iyo abantu baturuka muri izo ntara zitamba igisuru baje gushengera i bwami ari nko ku minsi mikuru yâ€™i bwami, iyo ntambo yaratambwa ku kirimba i bwami abantu bagatamarirwa. Niho i bwami hama hatambwa intambo zitandukanye kuko haza abantu bâ€™imihingo myinshi, bakaza bazanye intambo nâ€™utugenegene twâ€™i wabo.
Ubu iyo ntambo iratambwa mu mirwi ndangakaranga dusanga mu bice bimwe bimwe vyâ€™igihugu na canecane mu bisagara. Iyo bazitamba, ntibaraba ngo bakomoka mu ntara zahora ziyitirirwa gusa. Itambwa na bose.
Ufise ico utwunganirako, twandikire aha hepfo canke kuri akanyaburunga@gmail.com.

## Kubera iki mu biranga umusi mukuru wa Pasika harimwo amagi asize amabaraÂ ?
**Date:** April 20, 2025 9:50 pm  
**URL:** https://akanyaburunga.wordpress.com/2025/04/20/kubera-iki-mu-biranga-umusi-mukuru-wa-pasika-harimwo-amagi-asize-amabara/

Ntibimenyerewe hano iwacu, ariko mu migenzo yâ€™ibindi bihugu na canecane ibigwiriyemwo abakirisu nâ€™abayahudi, umusi wa Pasika uzwi nkâ€™umusi mukuru wâ€™amagi. Kuri uwo musi, abana bahabwa utuganuke tubanezereza twâ€™ibibumbano bisa nâ€™amagi dusize amarangi atandukanye. Muti ivyo vyoba vyavuye kuki?
â€œPessaâ€™hâ€, ijambo ryâ€™igiheburayo risigura â€œkujabukaâ€, ari yo Pasika mu Kirundi, ni umusi mukuru uhimbazwa nâ€™abakirisu hamwe nâ€™abayahudi kwâ€™isi yose. Mu Burundi, uwo musi watanguye guhimbazwa inyuma yâ€™umuzo wâ€™abazungu mu ntango yâ€™ikinjana ca mirongo ibiri.
Ku Bakirisu, ni umusi wo guhimbaza izuka rya Yezu Kristu (canke Yesu Kristo), nâ€™ukwitanga kwiwe ngo akize isi. Naho ku Bayahudi, uwo musi ni akaryo ko guhimbaza ukubohoka kwâ€™Abayahudi bari bafashwe ruja na Farawo muri Egiputa, maze bakajabuka ikiyaga gitukura bagasubira mu gihugu câ€™isezerano.
Eka nâ€™abapagani bÄƒrahimbaza umusi nkâ€™uwo kuva kera cane.Â Kuri bo, kwari uguhimbaza ihinduka ryâ€™ibihe, bava mu gihe gikanye cane baja mu gishushe. Aho akazuba kaba kagarutse, ibiterwa bigasubira gutotahara. Haba ari mu gihe ciza gishira iremba.

## â€œGiciyeâ€Â : haca igikiÂ ? Iryo jambo risiguraÂ iki?
**Date:** March 8, 2024 9:17 pm  
**URL:** https://akanyaburunga.wordpress.com/2024/03/08/giciye-haca-igiki-iryo-jambo-risigura-iki/

Mu mvugo yâ€™Ikirundi, na canecane mu mvyino zâ€™agahogo kâ€™abarundi, turamenyereye kwumva mu bitero bashiramwo ngo â€œ ngende giciyeâ€, â€œturagenda giciyeâ€, â€¦. Abarutse ubu riradusiga, kuko hari nâ€™ayandi majambo tudashoka dutahura avugwa mu Kirundi. None iryo jambo ryoba risigura iki? Ico gica coco ni igiki? Tubasabikanirize insiguro twahawe nâ€™abakurambere twayaze.
Ku batararyomva, bokwumviriza uruvyino rwakunzwe cane rwâ€™umugwi ndangakaranga Higa, rwavyinywe nâ€™abana bakiri bato ico gihe rwitwa Yoronimu. Muri urwo ruvyino, iryo jambo ryarakoreshejwe. No mu ruvyino rwa Giramahoro, Ngoma ya Ruhinda, iryo jambo ryarakoreshejwe.
Uwatumye dukora aya matohoza kuri iryo jambo, ni uko hari uwagize amakenga ko barya bana mu buto bwabo batatahura amajambo bariko baravuga yose. Ko abarikoresheje boba baratahura insiguro yaryo, si co tuja kurabira hamwe. Bararirimvye, badutuma dukurira mu karanga kandi twumva akadiho kâ€™iwacu banabuza amajamboi amwe amwe adapfa. Mbega iyo batarikoresha tuba turiko tuganira kuki?
None ico gica ni igiki?
Mu Burundi, ibikorwa bihuza abantu bakaja hamwe nko kuvyina no gutamba, bisanzwe bihabwa ikibanza kinini cane mu biruhura umuntu naho yoba afise ikimudundumiye ku mutima. Aho hambere rero, abantu barÄƒrama ku nama abakiri bato bagatamba cane bidagadura, bakikura ibinyugunyugu cane.
No mu migirwa yo kubandwa no guterekera, ivyigwa vyarerekanye ko hari ibintu vyafasha umuntu atamerewe neza afise ibigummbagumba canke ibiroroge vyamurengeye, bamubandiwe bikagabanya uburemere, agakira.
Ntiwtokwibagira kandi ko Abarundi baha ikibanza kinini kuyaga, kunywana bimwe bikwiye, ivyo bigatumwa no kugenderanira, baranayamaze ko agafuni kabagara ubumwe ari akarenge.
â€œIkigumbagumbaâ€ canke â€œikirorogeâ€
Ku bwâ€™umukurambere twayaze, ico gica rero ni ikigumbagumba kiba canize umuntu, iyo yidagaduye rero bikwiye abishizeko umutwe nâ€™umutima, nta kibuza ko gica, akumva icari ku mutima kirururutse. Icari kimudundumiye kubera kubura uwo mwanya wo kwidagadura, ushobora kuba ari umwitwarariko nâ€™ibindi, bica bigabanuka umuntu akaruhuka. Baca bavuga ngo â€œkiraciyeâ€.
Aha, uwoturusha gutohoza yotubariza ko hamwe bavuga ngo turabica bicike vyoba babikuye ngâ€™aho. Nta kiravyemeza dufise kuko uwo mukurambere twayaze we yaravyemeje ariko akekeranya.
Ikindi kivugwa, ni ikiroroge. Muti ico naco ni igikiÂ ? Ni urukumbuzi rwa cane, inkumbu nyinshi ugirira icuti canke umuvukanyi. Iyo zabaye umiurengera, zirahagarara ku mutima wâ€™umuntu akumva umenga zigiye kumuniga. Niho mu mvyino Â zindi twumva ibitero ngo â€œikiroroge kiranigaâ€.
Abandi nabo bati ni â€œigicuguâ€
Uwundi mukurambere nawe avuga ko nyabuna ikivugwa muri iyo mvugo ari igicugu. Ico naco ni igihe câ€™umusi kiri mu mwanya wâ€™ijoro, igihe kirenganye abantu baca batangura kuvyuka bifatira ingendo kugira izuba rimene ijuru banzaganije imisozi. Abo baba ari abafise ingendo. Uwo, avuga ko muri izo mvyino zose, bavuga ko baterama bagataha igicugu giciye, muri make, batahe bukeye kubera bahimbawe.
Nkako, mu ruvyino â€œIyo ntambaâ€ rwâ€™umugwi ndangakaranga Giramahoro, hoho baratomora neza mu gatero kagira indwi, bavuga bati: â€œigicugu kiraciye, ntamba weâ€. Aho turumva neza rukozi rwakoreshejwe ko ari igicugu cavuzwe.
Izo nsiguro zose uzumvirije usanga ari zo, ku buryo womenga ni rya jambo rimwe risigura menshi. Ariko iritomoye neza ryoba ryoroshe gutahurika ni irivuga igicugu kuko aho hambere abantu bagiye kuramukanya, baranywa bagatamba, bagataha bukeye canke butanguye kwenzura. Kira noneho, nâ€™ikiyago kibaye kirekire kiba caryoshe, iyo hariko hayaga abasanganywe: incuti, abavukanyi, umwana na nyina.

## Ukuresha kwâ€™aho hambere: akamaroÂ kâ€™akabuyeâ€¦
**Date:** February 13, 2019 12:25 pm  
**URL:** https://akanyaburunga.wordpress.com/2019/02/13/ukuresha-kwaho-hambere-akamaro-kakabuye/

Ubuhinga bwa none bwaroroheje ibintu vyinshi. No kuresha birimwo. Mwari muzi ukuntu aho hambere vyari bigoye? Nâ€™igihe ibintu vyo kuzanira abageni abahungu biviriyeho, kuresha vyagumye bigoye; ari agahambaye. Umviriza amakuba bacamwo kugira batebe bashike aho barushinga.

## #Inkingi zâ€™akaranga: Ntiharirizwa Innocent, ruremeshangabo mu mugwi ndangakaranga â€œAmagabaâ€
**Date:** October 3, 2018 5:50 pm  
**URL:** https://akanyaburunga.wordpress.com/2018/10/03/inkingi-zakaranga-ntiharirizwa-innocent-ruremeshangabo-mu-mugwi-ndangakaranga-amagaba/

Afise ijwi ridasanzwe. Ahibongoje abantu bata amacumu. Iyo ari mu giteramo ntawutaha kitarangiye kuko atosiga iyo ntarambira yandamye kunezereza abatumire. Imvyino ziwe zifise akanovera kadasanzwe kandi zimaze gutahukana ubushimwe bwinshi. Uwo ni Innocent Ntiharirizwa batazira Busokoza umunyakaranga ari mu mugwi ndangakaranga Amagaba. Menya vyinshi kuri iyo ntwari yâ€™akaranga.
Ntiharirizwa I.
Uwo muvyinyi, umwanditsi akaba nâ€™umutimbo yataye uruzogi muri komine Ndava yâ€™intara ya Mwaro. Ni ingabirano ku bavyeyi Ndayisenga Christophe na Bimazubute Euphemie. Yakuriye mu gisagara ca Bujumbura ku musase wa Mukaza aho yakuze abona mu micungararo abahungu bavuza ingoma akabikunda cane. Aho yakunda kuzibona mu kinanira aho bita â€œCentre Wallisâ€. Umutama juvent Sanganiye niwe yigisha abatimbo bakiri bato ari nawe yatumye uwo mukunzi wâ€™akaranga yinjira mu murwi wiwe Rukinzo Legacy aca akurira muri wo. Mu nyuma niho bamubwira ko afise ingabirano yo kuvyina, niko guca yinjira mu mugwi â€œAbaragwakarangaâ€ wari usanzwemwo abandi bagenzi biwe. Ibanga ryo kuvyina arikura aho.
Kuva akiri muto nâ€™igihe cose yariko avuza ingoma, na canecane aho atanguriye ibanga ryâ€™ukuvyina yagumye yiga nâ€™ibindi bicurarangisho vyâ€™ikirundi. Yize umuduri, ikembe, nâ€™ibindi. Abamwigisha ni abarigumije bemewe hano mu gihugu cacu. Abo nabo uwuza imbere ni mutama Torobeka Joseph yavyinye â€œJe Rufuku rwa Nganaâ€, Antoine (Kankundiye we), Cyrille, Baby John, Rurakomba wo mu Mabano na Gregoire twari tumenyereye avuza ikinanda (piano) nâ€™abana ku mboneshakure yâ€™igihugu. Abo bose aguma abashimira cane kuko bamufashije bidasanzwe.
Ishingwa ryâ€™umugwi amagaba
Ari kumwe nâ€™abandi bagenzi (imisore nâ€™inkumi) bakunda akaranga, bagiye inama yo gushinga umugwi ndangakaranga ufise intumbero tubona uno munsi ku mbuga koraniro nâ€™imboneshakure. Bipfuza gushinga ishirahamwe rimwe ryâ€™akarorero mu Burundi, muri Afurika eka mbere no mu makungu. Niko gushinga umugwi ubahuza bose mu ngabire zose bafise: amajwi atosoye, ubuhinga bwo kuvuza ivyuma, nâ€™ibindi. Batanguye ibikorwa igenekerezo rya 5 Rusama 2014. Mu minsi ya mbere vyaragoranye kubera ibihe igihugu carimwo ariko kuva 2016 nkâ€™uko Stephanie Soleansky yahora aserukira ikigo ndangamico câ€™abafaransa avyemeza, uwo mugwi ntiwasivye kwerekana ibitangaza mu kuzana dushasha mu karanga nâ€™umudiho wâ€™ikirundi.
Bariyumviriye izina bita uwo mugwi baca bahuriza kwâ€™izina â€œAmagÇbaâ€. Izina rikomoka kwâ€™igÇba, icumu baha samuragwa, ari naryo ryamye riranga abashingantahe. Ni rirya cumu riherekeza abatimbo canke rikabaja imbere. Kubwâ€™abo banyakaranga, igaba ni ikimenyetso cereka â€œubutore nâ€™ubutwariâ€. Kubera bari benshi baciye bitwa AmagÇba.
Umukozi adasanzweâ€¦
Abamuzi bemeza ko ari umukozi adasanzwe kandi ataruha. Baratangara ukuntu afatanya ibikorwa vyâ€™akaranga nâ€™ivyo kwubakisha inzu; ari navyo afitiye impamyabushobozi yaronkeye kuri Kaminuza yitiriwe Ntare Rugamba. Nkâ€™uko avyiyemerera, amaze kwandika imvyino zigera kuri 15 muri izo hakaba hamaze gusohoka: Amagaba na Burundi. Ubutwari bwâ€™iwe nâ€™ubushobozi buguma bugaragara mu bikorwa vyâ€™umugwi Amagaba, no mu giteramo â€œUmukozoâ€ ( Câ€™incuro ya mbere) yarerekanye ubuhinga budasanzwe aho yabonetse atamba ingoma, intore, avyina ,â€¦
Uruvyino Amagaba rwanitswe na Ntiharirizwa Innocent
Ngo ntibimugora kwiyumvira uruvyino. Bimuzamwo aho aba ari hose: mu muduga, mu nzira, aruhutse, eka umwanya wose. Imvyino ziwe zirimwo impanuro zidasanzwe kandi zose ziba zifise inkabuzo ikomeye ituma ayandika. Nkâ€™uruvyino Amagaba yarucishijemwo impanuro abakuru baha abana babo aho avugamwo amajambo sekuru wiwe yahora amubwira kera. Uruvyino Burundi rushasha yagomvye avuge ubwiza bwâ€™igihugu eka mbere anashiremwo amazina yâ€™abami yibaza ko abantu bariko basa nâ€™abibagira.
Yipfuza kubeshwaho nâ€™akarangaâ€¦
Uwo munyakaranga arashima cane intambwe umugwi yatanguje ugezeko aho abona bashoboye gukundisha akaranga kâ€™uburundi abanyagisagara bahora batakitayeho. Uno munsi arashima kuko benshi barabihurumbira. Ngo arizeye ko vuba nâ€™abaririmvyi bâ€™umuziki kizungu bazoteba bakabona akanovera kâ€™umudiho kirundi bakagaruka bagasohora indirimbo ziryoshe mu mayaya, urwedengwe nâ€™iyindi midiho. Mu vyipfuzo vyâ€™iwe, arashaka kubona atakindi kintu akora. Ashaka ko akaranga ari wo mwuga yotorana. Yipfuza guseruka mumakungu nkâ€™umuririmvyi (umuvyinyi) wâ€™umurundi akakigwa kumuntu adasanzwe.
Kugira ngo ashike ku co yipfuza, hari ibintu bitari bike bikenewe ari naho anegura abantu bataramenya akamaro kâ€™akaranga. Ku bwâ€™iwe, ntakindi abarundi babamwo abambere kwâ€™si atari akaranga. Niho aboneraho gutera akamo ababishoboye ngo biteho akaranga bimwe bihagije. Agasaba abantu batunganya ibiteramo bikomakomeye ngo baje baraha ikibanza akaranga. Atari abarundi bo nyene bahaye agaciro akaranga kabo, ntabandi bazobikora. Abategura amasabukuru bogerageza bagashiramwo imico yâ€™iwacu. Ngo amaradiyo nâ€™ibimenyeshamakuru navyo vyogerageza bigaha ikibanza kinini akaranga kâ€™iwacu no kugahayagiza. Nayo Reta, ngo yogerageza igafasha biboneka abariko barateza imbere akaranga.

Bakubwiye umwe aho ateramiye ata rungu aho ateye ikirenge harenguka akamwemwe, umwe atera ntateterwe ngo abure abitabira, yahibongoza ibinyanya bikanyaragasa binyeguruka mu bo vyizirikiyemwo bagataha biyereka; uwo si uwundi ni umunyakaranga Fabrice Nkurunziza yanditse yongera avyina imvyino yâ€™akanovera â€œ Vyagira muri bezaâ€ idasiba kuvuzwa mu manza zâ€™igihugu cose. Ngo wewe kuvyina no kwandika imvyino biri mu maraso, ntibimugora kubifatanya nâ€™ibindi akora nâ€™aho bigoye (akora mu vyâ€™ubuhinga bwa none ababizi barazi ko bisaba umwanya munini). Ariko we ntabiburira umwanya. Arashobora kuvyuka akavyukana uruvyino rushasha, akazi gaheze akarwandika rugasohoka ruryohoye cane.
None uwo munyakaranga ni nde?
Uwo aherutse kwubaka urwiwe yavukiye ku gacimbiri nyarumanga, ku muzozi Kiyange wa komine Gisozi, mu ntara ya Mwaro. Yize amashure matomato aho nyene i Kiyange aca abandaniriza ayisubuye i Nyakararo imbere yo kuja i Gitega kuri LycÃ©e Musinzira. Arangije yaraje i Bujumbura aho yarangirije amashure ya Kaminuza. Mu 2009 niho yatangura kuja mu vyâ€™akaranga aca yinyira mu murwi ndangakaranga Ihunja aho akiri nâ€™ubu. Akorera ikigo Amagara mu ngo nâ€™iterambere ( Village Health Works) kiri mu Kigutu I Vyanda mu ntara ya Bururi aho arongoye umugwi wâ€™imico nâ€™akaranga hamwe nâ€™ivyinkinoÂ  nâ€™Imicokama, agakora no mu vyâ€™ubuhinga bwa none.
Ibikorwa amaze gushira ahabona
Ibikorwa vya mbere yahereyeko nkâ€™uko abamuzi mu mashure yisumbuye na matomato babivuga ngo ni ugusubiramwo imvyino zaca ku maradiyo mi myaka yâ€™2000 akazishira mu majambo yabaryohera bari mwâ€™ikarashishi. Umwe mu bo biganye yambwiye ati: â€œTweho ntituzi ingene yabikora. Yarashobora kugenda aravyina tukagenda ibirometero bitanu vyose atawumwakiriyeâ€. Nâ€™igihe aziye i Bujumbura yarakunzwe cane kuko karyosha ikarashishi mu migwi itandukanye.
Ibindi bikorwa yabikoreye mu mugwi ndangakaranga Ihunja. Mu nkurikirane zose zâ€™uwo mugwi, imvyino za Fabrice Nkurunziza ni izi zikurikira: Vyagira muri beza, Soma rusose, Nyaruka urabe ihunja,Tubahaye mwiriye, Basasire izo ndava, Nzimanira abantu, Nkundira ndakwigine, Ducandagishe ibibondo, nâ€™izindi zitarasohoka. Â No mu kigo akoramwo ubu amaze gukora imvyino zitari nke. Aha twovuga: Village health works, Kari akaranga, Dukomeze indero, Amahoro azorama, Gupimisha imbanyi, Kurondoka ku rugero, Vumera, Dukomeze akaranga.
â€œBashitsi bezaâ€ canke â€œVyagira muri beza?â€
Urwo ruvyino rwarakunzwe cane. Na nyene kuruvyina ngo ni rwo akunda kurusha izindi. Amazu yâ€™imanza yose yo mu gisagara no hagati mu gihugu nta nâ€™imwe itarufise. Mu duhamagazo, mu mashini zâ€™abantu, hose urusangamwo. Benshi barwita Bashitsi beza ariko izina ryarwo ni Vyagira muri beza. Â Ngo ntirwamutwaye umwanya munini mu kurukora.
â€œUrwo ruvyino ndibuka ko narwanditse isaha icenda zâ€™ijoro nari nikanguye nca numva mvyukanye ingero nâ€™amajambo yerekeye ubukwe. Ico gihe nari ahantu hari amatara naciye mvyuka nandika ibitero bine naraye ndabimaze. Ibindi navyongeyeko bukeye ruca rurahera. Nta munsi rwantwaye.
Ko ruzoryoha naravyumlva kubera ingoga narukorana uwo mwanya muto narukoze narumva neza ko amajambo ariko arisuka yarayaryoheye ugutwi agashikira nâ€™umutima. Hagera mu ngero yarwo naho nkumva irarengeje. Sinatangaye cane kubona rwarakunzwe cane nâ€™ubu rukaba rugifise akanovera kadasanzwe ku rubuga.â€
Akamo atera abarundi
Uwo munyakaranga nâ€™ubu aracavyina. Arabandanya kwandika no gutunganya imvyino nshasha. Ngo aripfuza kuba imboneza mu kugarukira akaranga kâ€™igihugu, asasagaze umudiho kavukire nâ€™akanovera kawo mu gihugu no mu makungu. Anatera akamo abarundi ngo biteho kandi bashigikire ivyino kavukire bareke kwishinga iziva mu mahanga. Nabo abavyinyi ngo ntibadebukirwe kuko bitebe bitebuke uwo mwuga uzoteba ubatunge.
Ngo ikimubabaza ni uko ibikorwa vyâ€™abavyinyi (co kimwe nâ€™abanyatugenegene bose) bidakingiwe, abavyinyi ntibafatwe mu mugongo kandi ukamengo abantu nta gaciro baha umuziki kavukire kandi ariwo uduha iteka mu makungu. Aha agirako ashima itegeko leta isherutse gushiraho ryo gukingira ibikorwa mvabwenge agasaba ko ryokurikizwa mbere akipfuza ko leta yofata mu mugongo abakora umuziki kavukire.
Mu kubirindira abandanya ateramisha abantu mu gutwikurura no mu zindi manza, yivuga canke ahibongoza.

Ijwi ryawe twakuze turyumva kwâ€™iradiyo nkuru yâ€™igihugu cacu. Ijwi rirongorotse riryoheye ugutwi, akenshi ryama riherekeza amakuru iyo bugorovye. Uruvyino rwawe rutanguye kuvuga, ababanyi hamwe nâ€™abagenzi bararyoherwa cane. Rwapfa gutangura, bose bakegereza iradiyo nâ€™akamwemwe kenshi. Abatagira insamirizi baraja no kuyisembera bumvise utanguye guhibongoza na kagahogo kawe. Bukeye ku mitumba, wumva abato nâ€™abakuru baziherera inyuma bazisubiramwo.
Numvise ijwi gusa, nibwira ko uwo muntu ategerezwa kuba ari uwahezagiwe, ameze nezaâ€¦ Sinihenda kuko mu nyuma naramenye ko mu buzima bwawe wari umuntu ashwashwanutse, umugwaneza, akunda ikiyago, akunda guteramisha abandi na ntaryo. Waryosha ikiyago. Ni naco gituma bakugomwe ukaguma ukaja uraryosha ibirori vyinshi vyaba mu gihugu. Numvise ko washengeye numvise umubabaro mwinshi, numva Uburundi buhekutse. Burabuze imboneza mu karanga.
Wari akarorero keza
Sinovuga ngo niwe wantumye nitaho ivyâ€™akaranga. Sinzi iyo nabikuye. Bishobora kuba biva kuri Siokuru yavuga amazina yâ€™ubuhizi nâ€™ubu nkivuga canke ahandi; ariko mu vyantumye ndakabandanya, imvyino zawe zirimwo. Akanovera kazo katumye numva uburyohe bwâ€™agahogo kâ€™abarundi. Urukundo rwâ€™akaranga natanguye kurugaragaza mu 2006 ndi mu mashure yisumbuye. Aho ngiriye muri kaminuza, naciye ninjira mu mugwi ndangakaranga, aho hose imvyino tuguma tuzikoresha. Nta nkeka ko wari akarorero keza.
Ni umubabaro kuri jewe kuri jewe kuko ntashoboye kukubona ukiri muzima. Nari naripfuje kenshi kukubona nkakwibariza utubazo twinshi nari mfise ku bujanye nâ€™akaranga kâ€™Uburundi. Ko ariko vyari vyanditswe ntakundi vyari kugenda. Ariko ntaco nzoja ndumviriza Muteteri, nâ€™izindi mvyino udusigiye.
Turahomvye cane kubona Tube turarinjora (2008) Vol 1 kidakurikiwe nâ€™ibindi bitabu vyinshi. KO wari waradukunze ukabona koko ko â€œugutwenga bizana umunezero, umunezero ugatyorora umutima, umutima mwiza ukorosha ubuzimaâ€ ukaduha igitabu co gutwenza, ntitwari kukurambana. Birababaje kandi Â kubona ugiye utarabona ishirwa mu ngiro ryâ€™ingingo iha agateka abakora ibikorwa mva bwenge ngo ugire ico usaruye ku mpetso waduhetsemwo nawe.
Ugiye twari tukigukeneye ariko ntakundi. Ese umunezero wamye wipfuriza abarundi wokwama uranga abasigaye. Ukurinjora wagumye usasagaza kukama kuranga abarundi twese. Genda uruhuke nezaÂ !
